iha phuraï paṇḍu-bhāvō vāsāgama-bhaṅga-gahia-siharāṇa
aṇavaraa-visajjia-vijju-ruhira-dhārāṇa va ghaṇāṇa // GaüḍVa.640 [āryā]

iha siddha-sundarīṇaṁ thaṇāṇa ṇava-ṇaha-vaāṇa ṇivvaḍaï
āamba-rāi-lañchia-viitta-bhuavatta-lāaṇṇaṁ // GaüḍVa.641 [āryā]


[p. 97]
iha muṇivarāṇa ṇikkampa-ṇiyama-paḍibandha-sandhiālōā
jhāṇa-viramammi jāanti ṇavara maliṇāgiri-guhāō // GaüḍVa.642 [āryā]

iha mukka-pallalummuha-pasaṇṇa-mahisāvalōiā hōnti
sēla-siharantarijjanta-ravi-arā diasa-pariṇāmā // GaüḍVa.643 [āryā]

chāyā-ṇivvāvia-saddalāṇa bhaddaṁ diṇāvasāṇāṇa
ṇaara-viṇiatta-gōvī-parigīa-vaṇanta-maggāṇa // GaüḍVa.644 [āryā]

iha pallī-dhūmubbhēa-dhūsarijjanta-kuñja-ramaṇijjā
hōnti giri-aḍaa-daṇḍāṇisāgamārambha-gambhīrā // GaüḍVa.645 [āryā]

uaya-cchaviṁ muantō purāṇa-kari-danta-piṅgala-maūhō
iha sōhaïsiharāsatta-maṇḍalō jāmiṇī-ṇāhō // GaüḍVa.646 [āryā]

dhārāhisitta-ṇava-kandalāṇa iha tācalantimālāō
jaraḍha-kalaviṅka-gala-maṇḍalāhilīṇā jalaharāṇa // GaüḍVa.647 [āryā]

iha sō taruala-vasuāa-salila-sambhiṇṇa-kēsarāmōō
pariṇaa-kiṇṇa-surā-andha-gāḍha-mahurōviṇimmahaï // GaüḍVa.648 [āryā]


[p. 98]
paḍhamāsārē iha tatta-bhū-ṇivēsāĩ vaṇa-kuraṅgēhiṁ
dara-ghaḍia-muhaṁpijjantiagga-sisirāĩ tōyāiṁ // GaüḍVa.649 [āryā]

iha vellanta-dumujjhia-bhiṇṇa-vaō-aṇḍa-kalala-sīariṇō
vāanti mēha-sīala-dhūli-lavutthaṅghiṇōpavaṇā // GaüḍVa.650 [āryā]

ēē virāa-gōmaya-hariantara-bubbuā parivahanti
saddala-sandāṇia-sahara-cittalā pūra-vitthārā // GaüḍVa.651 [āryā]

iha dhārā-vicchōlia-phalaṭṭhi-ṇiggaa-kasāya-gandhāṇa
virala-bhamarāṇaghōlaï lacchījambū-tarualāṇa // GaüḍVa.652 [āryā]

ukkandalāṇa ghōlaï ihasēriha-dalia-kēsara-vaṇāṇa
gandhō ubbuddha-kalamba-sīalō sēla-kaḍaāṇa // GaüḍVa.653 [āryā]

iha salila-kiliṇṇāamba-virasa-mālūra-sāra-surahīṇa
jalaa-samayammi raṇṇāṇilāṇa ṇivvaḍaï sōhaggaṁ // GaüḍVa.654 [āryā]

ṇava-dhārā-paḍibajjhanta-rēṇu-parisāmalā thalī-maggā
dhūsara-hariṇa-khura-cchēa-kabburā iha virāanti // GaüḍVa.655 [āryā]


[p. 99]
avamēhāō vi maïla-candimā hōnti sōmma-pavaṇāō
salilandha-gaaṇa-dara-ṇivvaḍanta-tārāō raaṇīō // GaüḍVa.656 [āryā]

iha sā ummuddia-sinduvāra-maaranda-bandha-suhaāṇa
saraa-diasāṇa viasaï lacchī uggandha-kamalāṇa // GaüḍVa.657 [āryā]

ia saala-disā-aḍa-viaya-milia-mahi-maṇḍalēhĩ saccaviā
sēṇā-bhaḍēhĩ sē suhaa-saṁṇivēsā vaṇuddēsā // GaüḍVa.658 [āryā]

avi a—

ēē viratta-suracāva-virasa-viralāhilakkhia-cchāyā
mahisa-khura-cchēa-vihāvia-ppahā maṇi-aḍuddēsā // GaüḍVa.659 [āryā]

icchā-pariatta-laā-viāṇa-uddēsa-pīḍia-dumāṇa
chāyā saccia aṇṇa vva raṇṇa-pharusā uvavaṇāṇa // GaüḍVa.660 [āryā]

vibbhamavaīṇa bhijjantamalaa-parigūḍha-kēsaraṁ jāṇa
tāṇañcia vialaï iha laāṇa phala-pelliaṁ kusumaṁ // GaüḍVa.661 [āryā]

ōsaria-sihara-bandhā tahaṭhṭhiōvatta-bhitti-pabbhārā
bhavaṇocchaṅgā te ccēa vijala-vāvīṇihā jāā // GaüḍVa.662 [āryā]


[p. 100]
jāā tāo ccia taha-mahaggha-maṇi-rāsi-sabalia-kkhambhā
bhamira-bhuaṅga-phaṇā-raaṇametta-vihavāōvīhīō // GaüḍVa.663 [āryā]

iha kirataṁā pura-saṁṇivēsa-pihu-paṁsu-rāsi-parivēsaṁ
varisāsu paēsa-paāsa-khutta-maṇi-viddumaṁ ṇaaraṁ // GaüḍVa.664 [āryā]

ṇīrēṇu-bhāva-ṇivvaḍia-sāla-sura-saaṇa-tōraṇa-viḍaṅkā
dūrē vi pura-ṇivēsā iha āsaṇṇa vva dīsanti // GaüḍVa.665 [āryā]

pavilīṇa-kusūla-ṭṭhāṇa-pharusa-busa-paṁsu-thauḍiuddēsā
iha bhū-daviṇaṇṇēsaṇa-viiṇṇa-vivarā gharōvāsā // GaüḍVa.666 [āryā]

iha kāla-rūḍha-sīrāgamāĩ jāāĩ bahala-hariāiṁ
bhū-guṇa-visaṭṭa-mandāra-baddha-gahaṇāĩchettāiṁ // GaüḍVa.667 [āryā]

iha kārahīsu kallaṁ uṇṇanti va bhūsu sāvasāāsu
ārāmanti viṇimmahia-kamala-gandhāō va disāō // GaüḍVa.668 [āryā]

sāhāsubandha-parisēsa-rajju-vocchēa-virala-jara-dabbhā
dōlā-maggā uvaṇiggamēsu ēētarualāṇa // GaüḍVa.669 [āryā]


[p. 101]
avasaṇṇa-purāṇa-ṇarinda-kittaṇa-ṭṭhāṇa-sōṇa-cuṇṇāō
iha jara-bhuaṅga-sambhāviāō pēranta-bhūmīō // GaüḍVa.670 [āryā]

iha ṇijjia-kundōsīra-sāra-sahaāra-pāḍala-rasāiṁ
kamala-karavīra-bāvīsu gimha-tōyāĩ agghanti // GaüḍVa.671 [āryā]

iha viaḍa-mūlabandhā ghaḍia-silā-sañcayā parisarēsu
asamatta-ṇivēsaccia jaraṁ gaā su-purisārambhā // GaüḍVa.672 [āryā]

duggama-bhāva-ṭhṭhia-ṇāli-ghaḍia-ghaṇṭēsu tōraṇaggēsu
iha ajja vi uddēsā sambhāvia-bhūri-vihava vva // GaüḍVa.673 [āryā]

ā-sihara-pariṭhṭhia-bhitti-sañcayā galia-dāru-paḍibandhā
ihadūmantiva abbhantarāavā bhavaṇa-vitthārā // GaüḍVa.674 [āryā]

jaṇa-viṇihaṭṭhāyasa-kalusa-hīṇa-pāhāṇa-dēhalī-bandhā
agaru-dala-lahua-jara-dāra-dāru-saalā iha ṇivēsā // GaüḍVa.675 [āryā]

iha vihaḍia-piṇḍī-bandha-sandhi-parilambi-vāla-ṇimmōā
āyāma-pariṭhṭhia-vaṅka-viaḍa-liṅgā thalāhōā // GaüḍVa.676 [āryā]


[p. 102]
iha ciñciṇīṇa ghettūṇa karaalōlumpa-piṇḍiaṁ pahiō
kavalēi jaraḍha-kalaviṅka-pakkha-parikabburaṁ kusumaṁ // GaüḍVa.677 [āryā]

dīsantipaḍhama-pīḍhāṇibiḍāruṇa-lagga-paṅka-lēvāō
iha vihaḍia-bhitti-cchēa-ṇiggaā jajjariṭṭhāō // GaüḍVa.678 [āryā]

iha lavaṇuggama-parihīṇa-bhitti-valayattaṇēṇa dīsanti
ahia-viaḍāō pūraṇa-samuṇṇaā kūva-kōsīō // GaüḍVa.679 [āryā]

pīṇattaṇa-dara-pariṇāma-bhaṅga-parikasaṇa-maṇi-kavālāō
āhōaṁajja vi iha kahēntigahirāō ratthāō // GaüḍVa.680 [āryā]

iha kālēṇa samīkaa-talāa-suramandirāō dīsanti
dara-ṇiṇṇuṇṇaa-saṇṭhāṇametta-visamāo bhūmīō // GaüḍVa.681 [āryā]

ghara-gōlaa-dārōsaria-mūla-paḍibaddha-cuṇṇa-rēhāō
ēāōpāḍalāvaṇḍu-kupparā juṇṇa-bhittīō // GaüḍVa.682 [āryā]

iha gambhīrāanti va ahiālōāĩ jālaa-vihaṅgā
chāyāsu vi dara-pāvia-khambha-cchāyāĩ bhavaṇāiṁ // GaüḍVa.683 [āryā]


[p. 103]
diasē vi bhūa-sambhāvaṇāe ukkaṇṭayanti aṅgāiṁ
ṇīsaddāō vi iha jhatti ghaḍia-saddāōvaḍahīō // GaüḍVa.684 [āryā]

iha dūmanti vaphala-patta-lōha-pavirikka-tāla-khajjūrā
avalōha-paloṭṭa-jarārahaṭṭa-daṇḍā gharōvāsā // GaüḍVa.685 [āryā]

ciṇhōvalakkhiā vihuārambhōhura-ṇarinda-dīsantā
iha ajja vi santi mahā-ṇihāṇa-maggā parisarēsu // GaüḍVa.686 [āryā]

aghaḍanta-dhūma-raa-ṇiggamāō palhattha-bhavaṇa-viralāō
iha hōnti gāḍha-timirā cirēṇaraaṇīsuratthāō // GaüḍVa.687 [āryā]

ia tassa ciraṁ sēvāgaēhĩ vihaḍia-samiddhi-bandhēhiṁ
ṇia-ṇaara-saṁṇivēsā vēri-ṇarindēhĩ saccaviā // GaüḍVa.688 [āryā]

kiṁ ca jāaṁ—

pecchahaladdha-cchāyaṁimīe paḍivaṇṇa-dappaṇaṁ vaaṇaṁ
kamalaṁ vasamuha-ravi-bimba-cumbiaṁ phuraï ṇaliṇīē // GaüḍVa.689 [āryā]

uvvahaï daïa-gahiāharoṭṭha-jhijjanta-rōsa-paḍirāaṁ
pāṇōsaranta-maïraṁ va phalia-casaaṁ imā vaaṇaṁ // GaüḍVa.690 [āryā]


[p. 104]
kaṇṭhōsariekka-thaṇāvasatta-pia-bāhu-ghōlira-karaggā
sōhaï imā paattia-tumbī-vīṇā-viṇōa vva // GaüḍVa.691 [āryā]

daïa-gahiālaāvali-kalia-ṇaḍālaṁmuhaṁ vahaï
bahula-ṇisā dara-hīranta-paḍhama-kalamindu-bimbaṁ va // GaüḍVa.692 [āryā]

vaaṇa-ṇayaṇa-ppahā-ṇijjiāṇa ṇūṇaṁ imīe ēāṇa
sama-dukkhāṇa va jāō samāgamō canda-hariṇāṇa // GaüḍVa.693 [āryā]

ia ōāria-cāvammi jammi pāūsa-vilasiavvēsu
ṇivvaṇṇēi pariaṇō sēṇā-lalaṇāṇalīlāō // GaüḍVa.694 [āryā]

kiṁ ca—

jassa pahāra-dhuāṇaṇa-riu-gaa-gaṇḍatthalucchalantāṇa
tiasa-parimukka-kusumēsu ghaḍaï paṇaō mahuarāṇa // GaüḍVa.695 [āryā]

tassa magahāhivaïṇō imāṇa ramaṇīṇa vihasiujjōā
tuha bahala-jasa-cchavi-pellia vva ṇa ṇarinda dīsanti // GaüḍVa.696 [āryā]

ēāṇa phuria-sēvā-cāmara-pamha-paḍimēsu dīsanti
anto bhaya-pīāo vva bāha-dhārā kavōlēsu // GaüḍVa.697 [āryā]


[p. 105]
dhua-maa-paṅka-kaṇukkara-ṇihēṇa jāṇaṁkavōla-kuharāhi
kumbha-ṭṭhia-muttā-kiraṇa-pelliaṁ ṇīi timiraṁ va // GaüḍVa.698 [āryā]

tē tujjha jaya-gaïndā ṇarinda viddavia-vēri-vaggassa
ṇavara giri-kaḍaa-paḍipellaṇēṇatēaṁ viṇōanti // GaüḍVa.699 [āryā]

aha vā
ṭaṅka-muhāhaa-kaḍhiṇaṭṭhi-mukka-dhūma-cchalēṇa uvvamaï
taddiasa-pahā-paripīa-timira-paḍalaṁ va kara-jālaṁ // GaüḍVa.700 [āryā]

vōlēntiṇia-pamāṇāṇurūa-paḍibaddha-vāsara-kkhaṇḍā
ṭaṅka-cchēocchaliā sarīra-saalāṇa saṅghāā // GaüḍVa.701 [āryā]

dīsaï ghaḍaṇummilanta-vimala-dasaṇa-ppahā-parikkhittaṁ
taddiasindu-pavēsāvalagga-jōṇhaṁ va muha-bimbaṁ // GaüḍVa.702 [āryā]

vialanti kaa-raṇakkāra-ṭaṅka-vocchiṇṇa-kāya-ṇivvaḍiā
diṇṇa-suhaṁāsura-saṅgara-ṭṭhiā paharaṇa-cchēā // GaüḍVa.703 [āryā]

ia sō vi taṭṭhi-ghaḍaṇā-viuṇujjala-maṇḍalō diasa-ṇāhō
tujjha paāva-cchāyaṁ paripphurantō ṇapūrēi // GaüḍVa.704 [āryā]


[p. 106]
tuha dūrāvajjia-sēharāli-valaēhĩ kīraï paṇāmō
ōhura-ṇaḍāla-vialanta-bhiuḍi-bhaṅgēhĩva parēhiṁ // GaüḍVa.705 [āryā]

saccaṁ tumammi diṭṭhē ṇa santi tumhārisatti paḍihāi
ṇavara tuha daṁsaṇañcia ṭhavēi kālassa māhappaṁ // GaüḍVa.706 [āryā]

visamattaṇaṁ vivihiṇō ṇa tavēi tumammi ṇāhasambhariē
āsaṇṇa-pāusōpallavēi gimhō vi vaṇa-rāiṁ // GaüḍVa.707 [āryā]

jāṇa ṇiaccēa guṇā kiṁ bhaṇṇau tāṇa ṇigguṇā jē vi
tē vi guṇē tuhaavalambiūṇaguṇiṇo vva ṇandanti // GaüḍVa.708 [āryā]

saṁṇijjhēṇaṁ va sirīe tujjha dāhiṇa-bhuāvalambāē
aṇavaraamaṇiṭṭhiamēsa kaṇaa-varisaṁ karō muaï // GaüḍVa.709 [āryā]

sāhīṇa-muha-sahassō kiṁ va ṇa tā vāsuī pasaṁsēi
jaï taraï cintiumalaṁ guṇē tu ekkēṇa hiaēṇa // GaüḍVa.710 [āryā]

vihiṇā jāṇaṇaḍālēsuvilihiaṁ kiṁ pi visama-pariṇāmaṁ
tē tujjhapāa-vaḍaṇa-cchalēṇa vasuhāhiva phusanti // GaüḍVa.711 [āryā]


[p. 107]
ahisāraṇammi taṁ riu-sirīeṇisiāsi-ghaḍia-paḍibimbō
ṇīlaṁsua-saṁvīo vva sahasi sahasāhava-ṇisīhē // GaüḍVa.712 [āryā]

sāmaṇṇāĩ vi ṇāmakkharāĩ ṭhaviāĩ taï vivēammi
kittaṇamettēṇa vijēṇaphurasi taṁ ṇavara hiaammi // GaüḍVa.713 [āryā]

tuha dhārā-lagga-samōsaranta-kari-mottiattaṇā khaggō
āḍhattōvala-varisambu-vāha-līlaṁviḍambēi // GaüḍVa.714 [āryā]

aṇurāo tti pariaṇōkōva-huāsa-ppaha tti paḍivakkhā
āṇā-paāṇa muddāsu tujjha vindanti sindūraṁ // GaüḍVa.715 [āryā]

vāmēara-bhua-bhavaṇā kaha ṇu sirī vasau tujjhakhaggammi
muṇiaṁ dīsaï iha saṇṭhiāe sē tammi paḍibimbaṁ // GaüḍVa.716 [āryā]

ṇa vi taha lōassa guṇā ṇia-ukkarisēṇa pāaḍā hōnti
tuha saṁmāṇagghaviā vaccanti jahā pahu pasiddhiṁ // GaüḍVa.717 [āryā]

ṇa hu paḍhamañcia paa-vīḍha-ghaḍia-maulīhĩkāriō taṁ si
bhiuḍī-bhaṅgāyāsaṁ avarāha-bhaēṇa va riūhiṁ // GaüḍVa.718 [āryā]


[p. 108]
tuha pahu savatta-sīmantiṇīṇa acchinna-bāha-dhārāhiṁ
dīsanti samūlāō va lōlā lambālaa-laāō // GaüḍVa.719 [āryā]

jāṇaṁ ṇa purisaārō juvaïsamā tēsu kaha sirīramau
ṭhiabhāvamitthamahilā mahilāō kahampi kāmēnti // GaüḍVa.720 [āryā]

jhīṇā ekkē tu asimmi saraṇamaṇṇē gaātumaṁcēa
sēsā vi riū jalahiṁ kahiṁ pi kira kē vi paḍivaṇṇā // GaüḍVa.721 [āryā]

vaccanti ahōuḍḍhaṁaïnti mūlaṅkura vva puhaīē
bīāhi va ekkattō kulāhi purisā samuppaṇṇā // GaüḍVa.722 [āryā]

taralattaṇa-vaaṇijjaṁ lacchīe tumāe ṇavaraoppusiaṁ
tīe vi pahuttaṇaṁ vō pahu-dōsa-vivajjiaṁ diṇṇaṁ // GaüḍVa.723 [āryā]

vivarīaṁ va taï imaṁ vivēa-sārammi dīsaï ṇarinda
bhīō dōsāṇa tumaṁ tē uṇa ṇaṭhṭhā tumāhintō // GaüḍVa.724 [āryā]

saalēsuṁ cēa disāaḍēsu dīsanti dēva paḍilaggā
dhōa vva disā-gaa-sīarēhĩ vimalā guṇā tujjha // GaüḍVa.725 [āryā]


[p. 109]
bhuvaṇa-garuēhĩ tē tuha hīranti guṇēhĩ taṁ puṇō tāṇa
hīrasi guṇa-lēsēṇa vi suaṇō suaṇāṇa ahiō si // GaüḍVa.726 [āryā]

dia-bhūmisu dāṇa-jalulliāĩ kālammi jāĩuttāiṁ
tāĩ tuha ṇāha rōhanti sampaaṁ vihava-bīāiṁ // GaüḍVa.727 [āryā]

paṇaīsu guru-maṇōraha-sampatti-samuttuṇēsu saṅkantō
maṇṇē tuha tēṇa pahuttaṇē vi ṇa maōpaḍipphuraï // GaüḍVa.728 [āryā]

lahiūṇa tumāhintō dēntēhĩ iō taōṇaravaīhiṁ
sāhāhĩ va dāṇa-dumō ṇarinda tuha vaḍḍhiō dūraṁ // GaüḍVa.729 [āryā]

tuha riu-gaa-kumbha-kkhutta-ṇisia-tōmara-ṇihitta-vivarēhiṁ
viraēntisuhaṁ muttāhalēhĩ ramaṇīō hāralaā // GaüḍVa.730 [āryā]

avi a—

parighōlaïsiḍhilia-jālasutta-santāṇa-saṇṭhiō hatthō
peḍhāla-thaṇaharāaḍḍhi-kakkhaḍēvīḍaa-ṭṭhāṇē // GaüḍVa.731 [āryā]

vellahalaṅguli-kara-kamala-mukkalijjanta-jāliā-valayā
kucchi-cchēā chajjanti siḍhila-dara-diṭṭha-bhaṅgaṅgā // GaüḍVa.732 [āryā]


[p. 110]
gāḍha-kavāḍaa-dukkhuccuḍanta-ṇaharāi-lañchaṇō lahaï
dara-mēhujjhia-hariṇaṅka-bimba-sōhaṁ thaṇucchaṅgō // GaüḍVa.733 [āryā]

kaṇṭha-ṇirōhuvvaṇa-vittharanta-ṇīsāsa-tulia-ṇāsauḍaṁ
agghaï visaṇṭhuluvvella-vallarī-cihura-pabbhārō // GaüḍVa.734 [āryā]

maṇivalayāula-bāhagga-mōaṇuppaṇṇa-karaalāyāsaṁ
rēhaï lajjā-paḍiruddha-thaṇaharaṁ bhualaā-jualaṁ // GaüḍVa.735 [āryā]

ia garua-vaïaruttaria-kañcuō kuṇaï pahu paōsammi
sejjāruhaṇaṁ tuha laḍaha-vēsa-suhiōpiā-satthō // GaüḍVa.736 [āryā]

ia bandi-ṇandia-jayaṁgāhipurārūḍha-sēṇṇa-viṇṇāsō
jāō sō laḍaha-vilāsametta-vīsanta-vāvārō // GaüḍVa.737 [āryā]

avi a—

sambhāvia-citta-viāra-kāraṇāmarisa-tambira-cchāyaṁ
tahajhāṇa-ṇimillañcēa hōi phuriāharaṁ vaaṇaṁ // GaüḍVa.738 [āryā]

ummillaï thōa-tthōa-rōsa-rajjanta-dāruṇāvaṅgā
māsalia-savaṇa-bhuaïnda-raaṇa-kanda-ppahā diṭṭhī // GaüḍVa.739 [āryā]


[p. 111]
sāmāaï sēalavāhiutta-viṇiatta-bhūi-lāvaṇṇō
avihāvia-kaṇṭha-cchavi-vocchēōvaccha-pariṇāhō // GaüḍVa.740 [āryā]

vihaḍaï havvavaha-sihā-kaḍappa-pellia-puḍaṁ ṇaḍālammi
kaha-kahavi ṇibiḍa-bhiuḍī-vihaṅga-sampiṇḍiaṁ ṇayaṇaṁ // GaüḍVa.741 [āryā]

ia tiṇayaṇa-rōsāṇala-vilutta-dēhō vi kusuma-kōaṇḍō
jāsuṇisaṇṇau ajja viauṇṭha-bāṇo ccia jayammi // GaüḍVa.742 [āryā]

ālulia-vēṇi-lēhaṁ bhamiaṁ tāraṁ ca bhualaā-jualaṁ
ṇēvacchaṁ jāṇa vilāsa-kampiacchāĩ a muhāiṁ // GaüḍVa.743 [āryā]

tāṇa ramaṇīṇaṇaa-bāhu-bisalaāmaṭṭha-kaṇṭha-pariṇāhō
uvvahaï sō vilāsī ṇiāha-ṇēvaccha-vicchittiṁ // GaüḍVa.744 [āryā]

tēṇa sa pallava-bhaṅgaṁ cūḍāmaṇi-bhāvamataruṇaṁ tāṇa
ṇijjaï kusumaṁ ā-surahi-kēsaraṁ ṇava-kalambāṇa // GaüḍVa.745 [āryā]

ā-mēha-samaya-suhaāsambhiṇṇōvavaṇa-kēaa-suandhā
sīariṇō sē hiaaṁ haranti raaṇī-muha-samīrā // GaüḍVa.746 [āryā]


[p. 112]
kumuāvabōha-mahurāviralāgaa-mēha-khaṇḍia-miaṅkā
agghanti ṇisā asamatta-galia-salilāgamātassa // GaüḍVa.747 [āryā]

ṇīsāsā khaṇa-virahe phuranti ramaṇīṇa surahiṇō tassa
kaḍḍhia-hiaa-ṭṭhia-kusuma-bāṇa-maaṁrada-lēsa vva // GaüḍVa.748 [āryā]

sō dīsaï uhaya-disā-pahāviāṇanda-bāha-salilēhiṁ
tāṇa parirambha-pasaranta-bhualaēhiṁ va acchīhiṁ // GaüḍVa.749 [āryā]

avi a—

phalihacchōara-dīsanta-paṭṭhi-vēṇī-sihāō va sahanti
sahasā vali-bhaṅga-taraṅgiṇīhĩ jā rōma-lēhāhiṁ // GaüḍVa.750 [āryā]

sasimiva ṇavōiaṁ vihasiēṇa ahara-ppahāṇuviddhēṇa
sāsāmōa-milantāli-lañchaṇaṁ jāpaāsēnti // GaüḍVa.751 [āryā]

jā kaṇṇa-kisala-karaala-milanta-cala-tāraāhĩ diṭṭhīhiṁ
kandua-kīlaṁ vasa-sēsa-bāla-bhāvā paāsēnti // GaüḍVa.752 [āryā]

jā lalia-laā-līlaṁvēlambantisia-danta-kusumāō
sahasā mahuara-jālāamāṇa-ṇīlambarāvaraṇā // GaüḍVa.753 [āryā]


[p. 113]
jāō saï-diṇṇa-saṇṇejjha-maaṇa-pūāarā sarīrēsu
sarasa-ṇaha-mañjari-maaṁ rattāsōaṁ pivalihanti // GaüḍVa.754 [āryā]

jāō pasaṅga-pariggahia-hāri-hariaṁsuāpaāsēnti
rambhā-gabbhattaṇamaṇaha-pariaraṁ ūrudaṇḍāṇa // GaüḍVa.755 [āryā]

līlōṇaa-muha-andāṇa khaṇḍiāhara-ṇihēṇa thaṇavaṭṭhē
hiaaṁ jāṇa pāaḍa-vammaha-bāṇa-vvaṇaṁ phuraï // GaüḍVa.756 [āryā]

thaṇa-majjha-cchavi-tāraṁkuppāsantaramaṇaṅga-ṇāsammi
uddhaṁ va lōaṇaṁ tiṇayaṇassa bandīkaaṁ jāhiṁ // GaüḍVa.757 [āryā]

ṇaha-rēhā jāṇathaṇēsu sahaïrōmañca-khaṇḍia-ṇivēsā
khaṇa-viraha-bhīruṇōsīvaṇi vvaphuḍiassahiaassa // GaüḍVa.758 [āryā]

cakka-juēṇa va vammaha-rahassa piahutta-gāmiṇōjāō
thaṇa-maṇḍalēṇa parirambha-lambha-viaḍēṇa sōhanti // GaüḍVa.759 [āryā]

pecchanti jāō calaṇē campaa-kaliōvaāramujjhantē
kaṇṇuppala-pahara-bhayāgahie vvapaīva-mālāhiṁ // GaüḍVa.760 [āryā]


[p. 114]
daṁsaṇa-ṇivīamīsā-vasa-kūṇia-ṇayaṇa-pamha-bhāvēṇa
jā pañjariamiva piaṁ dharēnti avasaraṇa-saṅkāē // GaüḍVa.761 [āryā]

ahara-ppahā-darāruṇa-dasaṇa-maūhēhĩ thaṇa-visārīhiṁ
vammaha-vaṇa-bandhēhĩ va jāō saruhirēhĩ sōhanti // GaüḍVa.762 [āryā]

dīha-pihulattaṇēṇaṁ hattha-daḍhāveḍhaṇekka-joggāō
jāṇakaaggaha-taṇhaṁ dēnti balā vēṇi-mālāō // GaüḍVa.763 [āryā]

avaraddha-ramaṇa-paḍimaṁ pijā ṇhavanti vvagaṇḍavāsammi
aṇṇa-lalaṇā-pasaṅgāvakalusiaṁ bāha-salilēṇa // GaüḍVa.764 [āryā]

saïsaṅghaṭṭa-samujjala-kōḍiṁ kaṇaa-rasaṇaṁvimōēnti
pia-muha-ṇihitta-viasanta-lōaṇā jāō samayammi // GaüḍVa.765 [āryā]

jārōsukkampia-kaṇṇa-kusuma-raa-puñja-pūria-thaṇīō
avacuṇṇēnti va dara-rūḍha-saṇṭhiē vammaha-ppaharē // GaüḍVa.766 [āryā]

kampāō vahanti thaṇattha-hattha-raṇiraṅgulīya-hārāō
aṅgaṁ thāmēccia muhala-mēhalā-ṇēuraṁ jāō // GaüḍVa.767 [āryā]


[p. 115]
citta-maṇi-kaṇṇaūrāhividdha-vivihōvarāa-pamhēhiṁ
vaṇṇaa-tūlillēhĩ va lihanti jā ramaṇamacchīhiṁ // GaüḍVa.768 [āryā]

ekka-disā-paḍilakkhia-vimala-dasā calaṇa-ṇaha-maūhēhiṁ
jā lāvaṇṇa-paḍīo vvasahantiparimāsa-mauīō // GaüḍVa.769 [āryā]

piahuttaṁ jāṇa vilāsa-lōla-līlā-phuranta-pamhāiṁ
uḍḍēnti vataralia-pakkha-saṁpuḍaggāĩ acchīiṁ // GaüḍVa.770 [āryā]

āsaṇṇa-piaamāhara-ghaḍanta-phuḍa-dasaṇa-kiraṇa-bhāvēṇa
jā muha-rasāsavaṁ piva pianti līlā-muṇālēhiṁ // GaüḍVa.771 [āryā]

bālāsu tāsu ṇava-diṭṭhirāa-hīranta-hiaa-taralāiṁ
aṇubajjhantāiṁ va sēguṇēhĩsōhanti laliāiṁ // GaüḍVa.772 [āryā]

parirambhaṇa-cakkaliaṁsāmā-thaṇamaṇḍalaṁ urē tassa
pāvaï līlā-allaa-ṇihitta-ṇaliṇī-dala-cchāyaṁ // GaüḍVa.773 [āryā]

sēsa-guṇa-ṇirahilāsā rūvañcia sē piantitaruṇīō
kō vā aṇṇēsaïdamaṇaassadala-surahiṇōkusumaṁ // GaüḍVa.774 [āryā]


[p. 116]
vāma-kara-pelliōṇamia-mēhalā-ṇibiḍiaṁsuētassa
vīsamaï vilāsavaīṇa jahaṇa-bimbe khaṇaṁ diṭṭhī // GaüḍVa.775 [āryā]

hasiaṁ cabhāmiacchaṁmuhaṁ caṇava-baula-paṇḍura-kavōlaṁ
jahaṇamaṇibbhacchia-mēhalaṁ ca jīaṁ vilāsāṇa // GaüḍVa.776 [āryā]

avi a—

aṇukuṇḍalamāvivaïṇṇa-sarasa-kabarī-vilaṅghiaṁsammi
sīsammi kōsumo phuraï cāru-cūḍāmaṇi-ṇivēsō // GaüḍVa.777 [āryā]

uppusiāhara-pēranta-piñjara-ṭṭhavia-kuṅkumaṁ haraï
ṇaha-vilihia-kasaṇummillamāṇa-bhumaaṁ muhamburuhaṁ // GaüḍVa.778 [āryā]

parigaṇḍatthalamāsavaṇalambi maa-ṇāhi-paṅka-lēhammi
agvaï avaṅga-maggammi sarasamāsōamuttaṁsaṁ // GaüḍVa.779 [āryā]

antō-maṇidāma-cchavi-vicchuriacchaṁsuaṁ suhāvēi
thaṇavaṭṭhamuvari-vikkhitta-sabala-kusuma-cchaḍāharaṇaṁ // GaüḍVa.780 [āryā]

ia dara-cakkhia-maïrāṇuviddha-tambōla-parimalō haraï
aṇumajjaṇamāharaṇāvalambaṇōsē piā-satthō // GaüḍVa.781 [āryā]


[p. 117]
kiṁ ca jāaṁ—

sōmmāhēsu ṇisammaï diṭṭhī rāujjalēsu ramaṇīṇa
sārasa-vāvī-paripaṇḍurēsu sē dasaṇa-vāsēsu // GaüḍVa.782 [āryā]

ubbhijjaï jaḍa-bhāvāvarōha-daḍha-maaṇa-saṁṇivēsammi
aharammi sarasa-baulāhivāḍalā rāya-vicchittī // GaüḍVa.783 [āryā]

paḍhamaṁ chaṇa-maggia-vaïarēsu sañcaraï maṇḍaṇucchāhō
gahia-himāvaṇḍura-maruaēsupāratti-dāmēsu // GaüḍVa.784 [āryā]

parikavisa-bindu-mālāvasēsa-maaṇāhi-danture phuraï
vaaṇammimaaṅkārambha-pēlavākuṅkuma-cchāyā // GaüḍVa.785 [āryā]

saṅgalaïmarubaa-cchēa-sabala-viṇiutta-damaṇaa-dalāsu
lāvaṇṇaṁmalia-ṭṭhia-pisaṅga-kundāsu kabarīsu // GaüḍVa.786 [āryā]

ia raaṇī-bhaṅguggaa-piaṅgu-paḍivaṇṇa-sēharōharaï
sisirammi malia-maṇahara-pasāhaṇō sē piā-satthō // GaüḍVa.787 [āryā]

avi a—

phala-ṇiggama-paḍipellia-parisiḍhilālagga-maula-cuṇṇāiṁ
cūāṇa jhaṇakkārēi māruō mañjari-muhāiṁ // GaüḍVa.788 [āryā]


[p. 118]
cittālakkhia-mauluggamāṇa sāyaṁṇivēsia-jalāṇaṁ
gaṅghamaṇāmōaṁ sattalāṇa kālōvirallēi // GaüḍVa.789 [āryā]

āvāi māhavīṇaṁ vicchāya-pariṭṭhiekka-kusumāsu
ṇimmala-sōrahaṁ mañjarīsu phala-gaṇṭhi-jaḍilāsu // GaüḍVa.790 [āryā]

ia sē diṇēsu mahu-siri-pariṇāma-suhēsuuvavaṇa-ṇivēsā
ṇandanti paṇaïṇī-pariaṇassaṇaarōvarōhēsu // GaüḍVa.791 [āryā]

kiṁ ca—

pērataṁ-haria-kōmala-khajjūra-dalujjalaṁ kavōlāṇa
ṇayaṇanta-galia-bāhañjaṇāṇa ṇivvaḍaï lāvaṇṇaṁ // GaüḍVa.792 [āryā]

dara-maulaṇa-majjhōṇaa-taṇu-rēhāanta-dhavala-bhāvāiṁ
ēnti ṇava-sasialāhaṁantōtārāĩ acchīiṁ // GaüḍVa.793 [āryā]

thōamiva khāma-gaṇḍattaṇēṇa parilakkhiōṇṇaa-ṇivēsō
parivāaïkakkēaṇa-parāa-kaṇaujjalōaharō // GaüḍVa.794 [āryā]

dobballa-paṇḍurāṇa umhāruṇia-ṇava-kēsara-guṇāṇa
viralattaṇaṁ va thōvaṁuvēimuddhāṇa thaṇaāṇa // GaüḍVa.795 [āryā]


[p. 119]
ia tassa paḍhama-maaṇāṇubandha-paḍibaddha-muddha-bhāvāsu
diṭṭhī ṇihua-vilāsālasāsu vīsamaï bālāsu // GaüḍVa.796 [āryā]

aha tassa thira-bhuakkhambha-ṇimia-ṇīsēsa-bhuvaṇabhārassa
āsi kaïrāa-indhō bappaïrāo tti paṇaï-lavō // GaüḍVa.797 [āryā]

appāettiamettēṇa ṇavara virasō vi jassa paḍihāi
siri-kamalāuha-calaṇēhĩ kaha vi jaṁ gahia-bahumāṇō // GaüḍVa.798 [āryā]

bhavabhūi-jalahi-ṇiggaa-kavvāmaa-rasa-kaṇā iva phuranti
jassa visēsā ajjavi viaḍēsu kahā-ṇivēsēsu // GaüḍVa.799 [āryā]

bhāsammi jalaṇa-mittē kuntīdēvē a jassa rahuārē
sōbandhavē a bandhammi hārianda a āṇandō // GaüḍVa.800 [āryā]

ālekkhiaṁca sarasaṁ ca parisa-lōṇaṁ casāravantaṁca
thiramujjalaṁca chāyā-ghaṇaṁ ca gī-vilasiaṁ ca // GaüḍVa.801 [āryā]

āgama-vāā chandaṇṇuā a te bharaha-gōama-ppamuhā
ṇandantijamēvaṁhāsa-kāriṇōsāra-kaïṇō a // GaüḍVa.802 [āryā]


[p. 120]
bharia-savaṇa-ṭṭhiaṁ bhūri-kaï-guṇōvāsa-kaṅkhiṇō jassa
subhaṇiamahō ṇaanti va vimhaya-caliēhĩ sīsēhiṁ // GaüḍVa.803 [āryā]

tō sō goṭhṭhī-parisaṇṭhiēhĩ sappurisa-saṅkahāvasarē
bhaṇiō vimhaya-viasanta-ṇayaṇa-vattaṁ viaḍḍhēhiṁ // GaüḍVa.804 [āryā]

dhārēi jalaharōhura-vasundharābandhabandhuraṁsēsō
kahavi viṇiuñcia-ṭṭhia-visaṭṭa-kaṇṭhaṁ phaṇā-valayaṁ // GaüḍVa.805 [āryā]

dīsanti jaa-viṇāsullasanta-ghaṇa-dhūmakēu-daṇḍa vva
jala-majjanta-disāgaa-khaṇuddha-dhariākarakkhambhā // GaüḍVa.806 [āryā]

ullasia-vīi-valayantarāla-pariattamāṇa-ravi-bimbā
hōnti savāḍava-jalaṇa vva gaaṇa-maggē vi maaraharā // GaüḍVa.807 [āryā]

vialanta-vijju-valayāpalayambuvaha-ṇivahā ṇivijjanti
taddiasa-pīa-salilā sāṇusaēṇaṁ va salilēṇa // GaüḍVa.808 [āryā]

jala-bhavaṇa-samālambia-sayaṇassa murāriṇō samuddēṇa
dijjaï mahā-paīvo vva vīi-saṁvelliō sūrō // GaüḍVa.809 [āryā]


[p. 121]
jāā vaṇṇāsāā aṇṇe ccia kēvi saṁvalantāṇa
chīra-surāuvva-viāra-visamiā saala-jalahīṇa // GaüḍVa.810 [āryā]

majjaï siharārūḍhāruhanta-puñjaïa-muhala-sura-lōō
kuhara-bharaṇa-kkamōsīamāṇa-jala-kalaalō mērū // GaüḍVa.811 [āryā]

calaṇanta-ṇivaḍiaṁsambhamēṇapalayambu-ṇibbhare bhuvaṇē
āruhaï raaa-ṇāvaṁ va tiṇayaṇō mauli-sasi-lēhaṁ // GaüḍVa.812 [āryā]

ṇāula-bhāvō jōāṇubandha-sañjamia-sāsa-pasarassa
pavvāliāṇaṇassa vi sayambhuṇō sāara-jalēṇa // GaüḍVa.813 [āryā]

iapalaya-jalapphālia-calanta-sura-sēla-vihala-vibuhammi
aṇahamavalambaṇaṁ ti-huvaṇassa jō jāaï murārī // GaüḍVa.814 [āryā]

jassa maha-dhūma-lēhā raviṇā sa-maūha-dāvia-dalēṇa
agga-ghaḍiēṇa dīsaï kavisekka-phala vva tāla-laā // GaüḍVa.815 [āryā]

tassa ira imō suvvaï viggaha-tuṅgāhihāṇa-paḍivaṇṇō
bhuvaṇammimahāsura-vaṁsa-vēriṇōaṁsa-ṇīsandō // GaüḍVa.816 [āryā]


[p. 122]
aha vā
ōsaraïsamuppaaṇā rahasa-ghaḍantaṅga-pellaṇa-vilōlaṁ
takkhaṇa-vihaḍia-bambhaṇḍa-saala-jālaṁ vaghaṇa-vaḍalaṁ // GaüḍVa.817 [āryā]

vihaḍanta-ghaṇa-vimukkā pariatta-vimāṇa-vañciā kaha vi
ṇivaḍanti galia-ṇia-piñcha-vibbhamā taḍiguṇa-cchēā // GaüḍVa.818 [āryā]

bhamiaṁ raya-vihuōahi-samucchalantēhĩ pakkha-sēlēhiṁ
sāhejja-saṅgaēhiṁ mahā-vihaṅgēhiṁ va ṇahammi // GaüḍVa.819 [āryā]

dīsaï vēugghāḍia-sāara-mūla-raaṇa-ppahāambō
paḍhamōvaïāruṇa-pellio vva maggō suvaṇṇassa // GaüḍVa.820 [āryā]

sōhantiamarisuggama-viuṇa-visāṇala-sihaṁviambhantā
dara-khaṇḍia-muha-ghōlanta-garula-vakkha vvabhuaïndā // GaüḍVa.821 [āryā]

mūla-phaṇā-maṇḍala-tahaṇisaṇṇa-ṇikkampa-dharia-mahiveḍhaṁ
sahaï ṭhiaṁ iara-phaṇāhiutta-garulaṁaṇantassa // GaüḍVa.822 [āryā]

vihaḍanti ṇaha-ṇivāā vihaṅga-ṇāhassakulisa-kaḍhiṇā vi
mandara-ṇihaṁsa-kiṇa-ṇiṭṭhurammi vacchammi vāsuiṇō // GaüḍVa.823 [āryā]


[p. 123]
ṇia-suṅkārōsāria-ṇa-paḍanta-vihaṅga-ṇāha-saṁsaggā
phaṇiṇō vihala-muha-cchōha-viuṇa-rōsaṁvisūrēnti // GaüḍVa.824 [āryā]

sambhama-calanta-diggaa-ghōlāvia-sāsa-muhala-karadaṇḍaṁ
sēsaṭṭha-bhuaa-kula-ṇāmiaṁ va ōsaraï pāālaṁ // GaüḍVa.825 [āryā]

ia ēsa vihua-visahara-samūha-sambhāviubbhaḍa-jasēṇa
bubbhaï viṇaā-taṇaēṇa sa-viṇayaṁ kaṇha-bhāvammi // GaüḍVa.826 [āryā]

avi a—

sambhama-bhamanta-vijjāharāsi-kēsara-karambiaṁ phuraï
uṇāuddha-ṭṭhia-cihura-daṇḍa-caṇḍaṁ va gaaṇa-alaṁ // GaüḍVa.827 [āryā]

uvvahaï bimba-ghaḍiaṁ tārā-ṇiaraṁ sasī viḍappassa
ṇiddaya-kavalaṇa-khuḍia-ṭṭhiaṁ va dāḍhā-kaṇukkēraṁ // GaüḍVa.828 [āryā]

rōsa-dhua-calaṇa-tēlokka-lacchi-vicchūḍha-ṇēura-cchāyaṁ
vivarāha-kēu-bhiṇṇaṁ ravi-bimbaṁ vialaï ṇahammi // GaüḍVa.829 [āryā]

atthakka-phuḍaṇa-vialanta-kalala-kalilaṁ va bāla-bambhaṇḍaṁ
ravi-bimbaṁ dīsaï kiraṇa-mukka-kīlāla-jambālaṁ // GaüḍVa.830 [āryā]


[p. 124]
taddiasa-muha-ṭhṭhia-lōha-kavala-kasaṇa-ppahā-vihiṇṇaṁ va
hēsanti rahasa-ṇivvūḍha-dhūma-kalusaṁ jaya-turaṅgā // GaüḍVa.831 [āryā]

ia taïā khaṇa-ṇivvaḍia-bhū-laā-bhaṅga-bhaṅgurāvaṅgē
jāē imammi bhuvaṇēsu dāruṇā āsi uppāā // GaüḍVa.832 [āryā]

kiṁ ca—

sarahasa-sañcāra-taraṅgiōru-taralāviō suhāvēi
ārasaṇā-guṇa-paḍibaddha-kuṇḍalō kusuma-pālambō // GaüḍVa.833 [āryā]

ghōlaïpaḍilagga-piyaṅgu-mañjarī-jāla-garuiaddhantō
asamañjasa-lāsāyāsa-pasiḍhilō kuntala-kalāvō // GaüḍVa.834 [āryā]

sahaï thaṇavaṭṭha-saṇṭhia-piṭṭhāaa-paṁsu-piñjara-cchāyaṁ
ahirāma-māhavī-maula-danturaṁ damaṇaāharaṇaṁ // GaüḍVa.835 [āryā]

paḍavāsa-paṁsu-dhūsara-dara-garuāanta-pamha-parisiḍhilā
ghōlaï mahu-maa-pariṇāma-virala-parivāḍalā diṭhṭhī // GaüḍVa.836 [āryā]

ia maaṇūsava-viasanta-bahala-kīlā-rasō suhāvēi
ēassa paṇaï-bhavaṇēsu ṇava-vilāsōpiā-satthō // GaüḍVa.837 [āryā]


[p. 125]
avi a—

lahu-visaya-bhāva-paḍisiddha-pasara-sambhāvaṇā-paḍikkhaliā
jassa samattā vi guṇā ciramasamatta vva dīsanti // GaüḍVa.838 [āryā]

aha vā
vasuhā-sayaṇa-pahuppanta-rēṇu-paribhōa-vihuria-kavōlaṁ
vayaṇaṁ hēmanta-miaṅka-dhūsaraṁ sāravēntīhiṁ // GaüḍVa.839 [āryā]

asamāraṇa-mūlubbhijjamāṇa-pamhagga-maḍahia-ṇaḍālē
alaē ṇīsāsa-ṇivēsa-jajjarēsañjamantēhiṁ // GaüḍVa.840 [āryā]

jaha-taha-pusiaṁsu-kaṇāvalamba-mantharia-pamha-parivēsaṁ
dēntīhĩ ahiṇavāṇanda-bāha-sōmmummuhiṁdiṭhṭhiṁ // GaüḍVa.841 [āryā]

akkhitta-cuḍuppuddēsa-samahiāambamuvvahantīhiṁ
ajhasuramaharaṁ vēlakkha-suṇṇa-diṇṇaṅgulī-kisalaṁ // GaüḍVa.842 [āryā]

ia ēsa hiaa-ṇimmāa-vammahaṁ khaṇa-khalanta-viaṇāhiṁ
rahasamummuhīhĩdīsaï paḍivakkha-ṇarinda-bandīhiṁ // GaüḍVa.843 [āryā]

ia uṇṇaēṇa imiṇā jaha ṇiṭhṭhaviō purā magaha-ṇāhō
taha sīsantaṁ ēē tumāō ṇīsēsamicchanti // GaüḍVa.844 [āryā]


[p. 126]
aha vihasiūṇasaṇiaṁsō jampaï ṇivvaḍanta-sabbhāvaṁ
kaïyava-vimuhāiñcia hōnti visuddhāṇa hiaaïṁ // GaüḍVa.845 [āryā]

dhīrēhĩ hiaa-ṇihiā kaha vigamejjantisōa-saṁvēā
aṅgāĩ paharisō uṇa garuāṇa vi kiṁ pi taralēi // GaüḍVa.846 [āryā]

kaṇṭhēccia parighōlaï puṇaruttaṁpaharisāula-kkhaliā
apahuppanti vva mahaṁ vāā pahuṇō pasaṁsāsu // GaüḍVa.847 [āryā]

avi a—

antōvāsaṁ viaḍāamāṇa-phaṇa-maṇḍalōsamuvvahaï
pacchāccheppa-cchala-ṇinta-dīha-dēhattaṇā sēsō // GaüḍVa.848 [āryā]

chīrāanta-ṇaha-cchavi-calaṇa-viṇimmia-paōhara-caukkō
gūḍha-muhō kummo ccēa lahaï āvīṇa-saṇṭhāṇaṁ // GaüḍVa.849 [āryā]

paḍhamutthaṅghaṇa-ghōlāviuddha-ghōṇāuḍēṇa paḍivaṇṇaṁ
uttuṇḍa-taṇṇaattaṇamaïrāvēuṇṭha-kōlēṇa // GaüḍVa.850 [āryā]

dēha-parivāḍi-pīḍā-huṅkāra-taraṅgiōviṇikkhamaï
dhūmāantō pāāla-bahala-tama-sañcaoccēa // GaüḍVa.851 [āryā]


[p. 127]
pāālōara-maggammi bhiṇṇa-viṇivēsa-siḍhila-galiēṇa
vubbhaï sumēruṇā taruṇa-rōaṇā-sāra-sārecchaṁ // GaüḍVa.852 [āryā]

khaṇa-pariatta-sahāvattaṇēṇa dara-ṇiggaaṅkura-siho vva
vaaṇuddēsō līlā-kavalia-taṇa-danturō hōi // GaüḍVa.853 [āryā]

takkhaṇa-pīvara-pasaranta-duddha-dhārā-ṇihēṇa mūlammi
sakulo vva vihāvijjaïbhāruvvahaṇāarā sēsō // GaüḍVa.854 [āryā]

ia jēṇa sambhamārambha-gahia-gō-bhāva-vibbhamubbhantā
puhaīpuhaī-vaïṇā vilañchiāṇiaa-ṇāmēṇa // GaüḍVa.855 [āryā]

tēṇa vi imassatulaṇā ṇa sahaïsuhaanti kassa vā virasā
saccaria-vañciāṇaṁ sēsāṇa sirī-samullāsā // GaüḍVa.856 [āryā]

kiṁ ca—

jāṇa alaṅkārasamō vihavō maïlēi tē vi vaḍḍhantō
vicchāēi miaṅkaṁ tusāra-varisō aṇuguṇō vi // GaüḍVa.857 [āryā]

mōha-salāhāhĩ tahā pahuṇō pisuṇēhiṁ vēlavijjanti
jaha ṇivvaḍiēsu viṇia-guṇēsu tē kimpicintēnti // GaüḍVa.858 [āryā]


[p. 128]
sulahaṁ hi guṇāhāṇaṁsaguṇāhārāṇaṇaṇu ṇarindāṇa
aṇṇēsiavva-maggā kattō vi guṇādariddāṇa // GaüḍVa.859 [āryā]

taṁ khalu sirīe rahassaṁ jaṁ sucaria-maggaṇekka-hiaō vi
appāṇamōsarantaṁ guṇēhĩ lōō ṇa lakkhēi // GaüḍVa.860 [āryā]

ṇa sahantisīla-sāraṁdōsēviciṇantiṇaccia vivēā
dōsammi guṇāārē ṇavaraṁ pahuṇō ṇisammanti // GaüḍVa.861 [āryā]

lōēhĩagahiañciasīlamavihava-ṭṭhiaṁpasaṇṇaṁ pi
sōsamuvēitahiñciakusumaṁ va phalagga-paḍilaggaṁ // GaüḍVa.862 [āryā]

ṇiccaṁ dhaṇa-dāra-rahassa-rakkhaṇēsaṅkiṇō viacchariaṁ
āsaṇṇa-ṇīa-vaggā jaṁ tahavi ṇarāhivā hōnti // GaüḍVa.863 [āryā]

pecchahavivarīam imaṁbahuā maïrā maēi ṇa hu thōvā
lacchī uṇathōvā jahamaēi ṇa tahāira bahūā // GaüḍVa.864 [āryā]

jē ṇivvaḍia-guṇā vi hu siriṁ gaā tē vi ṇigguṇā hōnti
tē uṇa guṇāṇa dūrē aguṇaccia jē gaā lacchiṁ // GaüḍVa.865 [āryā]


[p. 129]
ekkē lahua-sahāvā guṇēhĩ lahiuṁ mahanti dhaṇa-riddhiṁ
aṇṇē visuddha-cariā vihavāhi guṇē vimagganti // GaüḍVa.866 [āryā]

parivāra-dujjaṇāiṁ pahu-pisuṇāiṁ pihōnti gēhāiṁ
uhaa-khalāiṁ tahaccia kamēṇa visamāĩ maṇṇetthā // GaüḍVa.867 [āryā]

ettiamettēṇa guṇē ṇaṇu paḍivajjanti ṇivvivēā vi
jettiamettēṇa pahū garuāṇa parammuhā hōnti // GaüḍVa.868 [āryā]

taha ayasiṇō guṇēhiṁ jāā suaṇājaṇammisaalammi
dōsāaraṇaṁ pi ṇa gāravāya jaha sampaaṁ tāṇa // GaüḍVa.869 [āryā]

gahiā guṇattaṇēṇaṁ phalanti dōsā phuḍaṁ ṇarindēsu
dōsaccia guṇa-sambhāvaṇāe jaïtāṇajāanti // GaüḍVa.870 [āryā]

mūḍhē jaṇammi a-muṇia-guṇa-sāra-vivēa-vaïaruvviggā
kiṁ aṇṇaṁ sappurisāgāmāōvaṇaṁpavajjanti // GaüḍVa.871 [āryā]

dukkhēhĩ dōhĩ suaṇāahiūrijjantidiasiaṁcēa
supurisa-kālē a ṇa jaṁ jaṁ jāā ṇīa-kālē a // GaüḍVa.872 [āryā]


[p. 130]
sumaīṇa sucariāṇa a dēntāālōaṇaṁpasaṅgaṁ ca
pahuṇō jaṁ ṇiaa-phalaṁ taṁtāṇaphalaṁ ti maṇṇanti // GaüḍVa.873 [āryā]

aṇṇō vi ṇāma vihavīsuhāĩ līlāsahāĩṇivvisaï
asamañjasa-karaṇe ccēa ṇavaraṇivvaḍaïpahubhāvō // GaüḍVa.874 [āryā]

andōlantāṇa khaṇaṁ garuāṇa aṇāarē pahu-kaammi
hiaaṁ khala-bahumāṇāvalōaṇē ṇavaraṇivvāi // GaüḍVa.875 [āryā]

patthiva-gharēsu guṇiṇō vi ṇāma jaï kēvi sāvasāsa vva
jaṇa-sāmaṇṇaṁ taṁ tāṇa kimpi aṇṇañcia ṇimittaṁ // GaüḍVa.876 [āryā]

vaccanti vēsa-bhāvaṁ jēhiñcia sajjaṇā ṇarindāṇa
tēhiñcia bahumāṇaṁ guṇēhĩkiṁṇāma magganti // GaüḍVa.877 [āryā]

ko vva ṇa paraṁmuhō ṇigguṇāṇa guṇiṇō ṇa kaṁ va dūmēnti
jō vā ṇa guṇī jō vā ṇa ṇigguṇō sō suhaṁ jiaï // GaüḍVa.878 [āryā]

jaṁ suaṇēsu ṇiattaï pahūṇa paḍivatti-ṇīsahaṁ hiaaṁ
taṁ khu imaṁ raaṇāharaṇa-mōaṇaṁ gārava-bhaēṇa // GaüḍVa.879 [āryā]


[p. 131]
avivēa-saṅkiṇo ccēaṇigguṇā para-guṇē pasaṁsanti
laddha-guṇā uṇa pahuṇō bāḍhaṁ vāmā para-guṇēsu // GaüḍVa.880 [āryā]

savvo ccia sa-guṇukkarisa-lālasō vahaï maccharucchāhaṁ
tē pisuṇā jē ṇa sahanti ṇigguṇā para-guṇuggārē // GaüḍVa.881 [āryā]

suaṇattaṇēṇa gheppaï thōēṇañcia parō sucariēṇa
dukkha-pariōsiavvōappāṇōccēa lōassa // GaüḍVa.882 [āryā]

mottuṁ guṇāvalēvō tīraï kaha ṇu viṇaya-ṭṭhiēhiṁ pi
mukkammi jammi so ccia viuṇaaraṁ phuraïhiaammi // GaüḍVa.883 [āryā]

dūmijjantā hiaēṇa kiṁ pi cintēnti jaï ṇa jāṇāmi
kiriyāsu puṇa paaṭṭantisajjaṇā ṇāvaraddhē vi // GaüḍVa.884 [āryā]

mahimaṁ dōsāṇa guṇā dōsā vi hu dēnti guṇa-ṇihāassa
dōsāṇa jē guṇā tē guṇāṇa jaï tā ṇamō tāṇa // GaüḍVa.885 [āryā]

suaṇāanti khalā vi hu suaṇā vi khalattaṇaṁ va dāvēnti
ēso ccia sīmantō guṇāṇaṁ dūraṁ phurantāṇa // GaüḍVa.886 [āryā]


[p. 132]
saṁsēviūṇa dōsē appā tīraïguṇa-ṭṭhiōkāuṁ
ṇivvaḍia-guṇāṇa puṇō dōsēsu maī ṇa saṇṭhāi // GaüḍVa.887 [āryā]

suṭṭhu vi parihīṇa-guṇō suaṇō aṇṇēhĩ hōi sāmaṇṇō
sahaārē galia-rasē vi bhūa-kajjaṁ ṭhiaṁ cēa // GaüḍVa.888 [āryā]

kalahōāimayāiṁ ṇavaraṁ mahilāṇa dappaṇa-alāiṁ
purisāṇa dappaṇaṁ caria-dhāriṇōsajjaṇaccēa // GaüḍVa.889 [āryā]

vaaṇa-vimukkaṁ pi khalō aṇṇattō dāruṇattaṇaṁvahaï
dhārāsu muhuttiṇṇaṁ pidharaïpharusattaṇaṁ dabbhō // GaüḍVa.890 [āryā]

parigaa-paraguṇa-sārattaṇēṇa viuṇaṁ visūramāṇāṇa
hōi vivēo ccia dujjaṇāṇa pisuṇattaṇa-ṇimittaṁ // GaüḍVa.891 [āryā]

aha mōhō para-guṇa-lahuaāe jaṁ kira guṇāpayaṭṭanti
appāṇa-gāravañcia guṇāṇa garuattaṇa-ṇimittaṁ // GaüḍVa.892 [āryā]

vubbhantē jammi guṇuṇṇaā vi lahuattaṇaṁ va pāvēnti
kaha ṇāma ṇigguṇaccia taṁ vahanti māhappaṁ // GaüḍVa.893 [āryā]


[p. 133]
māhappēguṇa-kajjammi aguṇa-kajjēṇibaddha-māhappā
vivarīaṁ uppattiṁ guṇāṇa icchanti kāvurisā // GaüḍVa.894 [āryā]

guṇa-sambhavō maōsupurisāṇa saṅkamaïṇēahiaammi
tēṇaaṇivvūḍha-maa vva tāṇa garuā guṇā hōnti // GaüḍVa.895 [āryā]

tā cēa macchara-malaṁjāva vivēōphuḍaṁ ṇavipphuraï
jaliaṁ ca bhaavaā huavahēṇa dhūmō a viṇiattō // GaüḍVa.896 [āryā]

tuṅgāvalōaṇē hōi vimhaō ṇīa-daṁsaṇē saṅkā
jaha pecchantāṇa giriṁ jahēa avaḍaṁ ṇiantāṇa // GaüḍVa.897 [āryā]

icchāmi vimukka-guṇaṁ pisuṇāsaṅkāe kāumappāṇaṁ
visahara-saṅkhōhukkhitta-kusuma-mālaṁ va raaṇīē // GaüḍVa.898 [āryā]

jaṇamaṇahigīaguṇagāravaṁ pi guṇa-gavviaṁ ṇiēūṇa
bhuvaṇārūḍha-guṇāṇa vi appā andōlaï guṇēsu // GaüḍVa.899 [āryā]

guṇiṇō vihavārūḍhāṇa vihaviṇō guru-guṇāṇa ṇa hu kimpi
lahuanti va aṇṇōṇṇaṁ girīṇa jē mūla-siharēsu // GaüḍVa.900 [āryā]


[p. 134]
ṇa tahāmahāguṇēsumāhappadharā havanti ṇaravaïṇō
sāhaṅkārā jaha patthivēsu te ccēa dīsanti // GaüḍVa.901 [āryā]

jaha jaha ṇagghanti guṇā jaha jahadōsā asampaï phalanti
aguṇāarēṇa taha taha guṇa-suṇṇaṁ hōhii jaaṁ pi // GaüḍVa.902 [āryā]

kiṁ va ṇarindēhĩ vivēa-mukka-saalāhilāsa-ṇīsaṅgā
vihiṇō vidhīra-paḍibaddha-pariarāhōnti sappurisā // GaüḍVa.903 [āryā]

thōārambhē vi vihimmi āyasagge vva khaṇḍaṇamuvēnti
sa-paripphandēṇañcia ṇīābhami-dāru-saalaṁ va // GaüḍVa.904 [āryā]

viṇṇāṇālōo cciakumaīṇavisāraaṁpaāsēi
kasaṇāṇa maṇīṇaṁpiva tēa-pphuraṇaṁsiaṁcēa // GaüḍVa.905 [āryā]

hiaa-viaḍattaṇēṇaṁ garuāṇa ṇa ṇivvaḍanti buddhīō
ghōlanti mahā-bhavaṇēsu manda-kiraṇaccia paīvā // GaüḍVa.906 [āryā]

accanta-viēēṇa vi garuāṇa ṇa ṇivvaḍanti saṅkappā
vijjujjōō bahalattaṇēṇa mōhēi acchīiṁ // GaüḍVa.907 [āryā]


[p. 135]
jēgēṇhantisayañcia lacchiṁ ṇa hu tē ṇa gārava-ṭṭhāṇaṁ
tē uṇa kēvi sayañciadāliddaṁgheppaē jēhiṁ // GaüḍVa.908 [āryā]

ekkē pāvanti ṇa taṁ aṇṇēparao vvatīe dīsanti
iarāṇa mahagghāṇaṁ ca antarē ṇivasaï pasaṁsā // GaüḍVa.909 [āryā]

maraṇamahiṇandamāṇāṇa appaṇaccēa mukka-vihavāṇa
kuṇaïkuviōkaantō jaï vivarīaṁsu-purisāṇa // GaüḍVa.910 [āryā]

uvaaraṇībhūa-jaā ṇa hu ṇavara ṇa pāviā pahu-ṭṭhāṇaṁ
uvaaraṇaṁ pi ṇa jāā guṇa-guruṇō kāla-dōsēṇa // GaüḍVa.911 [āryā]

chāyā sā ira maṇṇē aṇantarāgāmiṇō kaa juassa
kali-kāla-bharammi vi kimpi jēṇa vimalaṁpaḍipphuraï // GaüḍVa.912 [āryā]

visaïccēasarahasaṁjēsuṁ kiṁ tēhĩ khaṇḍiāsēhiṁ
ṇikkhamaï jēsupariōsa-ṇibbharōtāĩ gēhāiṁ // GaüḍVa.913 [āryā]

ujjhaïuāra-bhāvaṁdakkhiṇṇaṁ karuṇaaṁ caāmuaï
kāṇa visamōsarantīchippaï puhavī vipāvēhiṁ // GaüḍVa.914 [āryā]


[p. 136]
anto ccia ṇihuaṁ vihasiūṇa acchantivimhiātāhē
iara-sulahaṁ pi jāhē garuāṇa ṇa kimpi sampaḍaï // GaüḍVa.915 [āryā]

dāvēnti sajjaṇāṇaṁ icchā-garuaṁpariggahaṁ garuā
maaṇa-viṇivēsa-diṭṭhaṁ mahā-maṇīṇaṁ va paḍibimbaṁ // GaüḍVa.916 [āryā]

sāhīṇa-sajjaṇā vi hu ṇīa-pasaṅgē ramanti kāurisā
sā ira līlā jaṁ kāa-dhāraṇaṁ sulaha-raaṇāṇa // GaüḍVa.917 [āryā]

thāma-tthāma-ṇivēsia-sirīṇa garuāṇa kaha ṇu dāliddaṁ
ekkā uṇakiviṇa-sirī gaā a mūlaṁ ca pamhusiaṁ // GaüḍVa.918 [āryā]

kiviṇāṇa aṇṇa-visaē dāṇa-guṇē ahisalāhamāṇāṇa
ṇia-cāē ucchāhō ṇa ṇāma kaha vā ṇa lajjā vi // GaüḍVa.919 [āryā]

parihōa-sahāṇavavahuvva tāṇa ṇava-saṅgamālasā lacchī
iarā lahiūṇa siriṁ ṇa kāma-līlā-parātēṇa // GaüḍVa.920 [āryā]

acchanticcia kiviṇā achivantā pāsa-gōaraṁ lacchiṁ
parihāravaïṁ va piyaṁmaïla-cchāyaṁṇiacchantā // GaüḍVa.921 [āryā]


[p. 137]
paramattha-pāvia-guṇāgaruaṁ pi hu palahuaṁ vamaṇṇanti
tēṇa sirīe virōhō guṇēhĩ ṇikkāraṇaṁ ṇa uṇa // GaüḍVa.922 [āryā]

bhumaā-bhaṅgāṇattā visuvurisaṁjaṁ ṇa turiamalliaï
taṁ maṇṇe dhāvantī rahasēṇa sirī parikkhalaï // GaüḍVa.923 [āryā]

ṇaṇu ṇāsamaṇavalambā ēiccia sā vi suvurisābhāvē
devva-vasātēṇasirīe hōi ṇāsaṁsiō virahō // GaüḍVa.924 [āryā]

dhamma-pasūā kaha hōu bhaavaīvēsa-sajjaṇā lacchī
tāō alacchio ccia lacchi-ṇihā jā aṇajjēsu // GaüḍVa.925 [āryā]

jā viulājāōciraṁ jā parihōḍajjalāō lacchīō
āāradharāṇaṁcia tāō ṇauṇō aiarāṇa // GaüḍVa.926 [āryā]

avaṇēi dēi a guṇē dōsēṇūmēidēi a paāsaṁ
dīsaï ēsa viruddho vva kō vi lacchīe viṇṇāsō // GaüḍVa.927 [āryā]

samare dhārā-gōaramuvēnti jēvaïri-maṇḍalaggāṇa
tē tammi balā khalu ṇivasirīe lacchīechippanti // GaüḍVa.928 [āryā]


[p. 138]
apphōḍaṇāhighāa-cchalēṇa ciramekka-bhua-kaāsaṅghā
viṇivārēnti va vīaṁbhuaṁ pi dappēṇasappurisā // GaüḍVa.929 [āryā]

aṇṇōṇṇaṁ lacchiguṇāṇaṇūṇapisuṇā guṇaccia ṇa lacchī
lacchīahilēi guṇē lacchiṁṇa uṇō guṇā jēṇa // GaüḍVa.930 [āryā]

lacchī-laāe mūlaṁ guṇatti ēaṁ pariṭṭhiañcēa
jēṇa ahō-gamaṇañcēa tāṇa parivaḍḍhaṇē tīē // GaüḍVa.931 [āryā]

ayasaṁ dāūṇa visaṇṭhulāṇa sajjhasa-visūriavvāṇa
paḍhamañcia jīe paāĩ mahumahe ccēa khaliāiṁ // GaüḍVa.932 [āryā]

sā caḍulā kaha ṇu guṇujjalēsu lacchī akūṇiaṁkuṇau
ciraālōsia-pāāla-timira-saṁvāhiaṁ diṭṭhiṁ // GaüḍVa.933 [āryā]

jīe samārambhe ccia lacchī paḍhama-ṭṭhiā vi vivalāi
aṇṇā tīe ccia patthaṇāe kaha ṇāma saṅghaḍaï // GaüḍVa.934 [āryā]

dukkhābhāvō ṇa suhaṁ tāĩ vi ṇa suhāĩ jāĩsokkhāiṁ
mottūṇa suhāĩ suhāĩ jāĩ tāĩccia suhāiṁ // GaüḍVa.935 [āryā]


[p. 139]
suha-saṅga-gārave cciahavanti dukkhāĩdāruṇaarāiṁ
ālōukkarise cciacchāyābahalattaṇam uvēi // GaüḍVa.936 [āryā]

suha-saṅgōsuha-viṇivattiekka-cittāṇa aviraaṁ phuraï
aṅguli-pihiāṇa ravōavvocchiṇṇo vva kaṇṇāṇa // GaüḍVa.937 [āryā]

dūmijjantāĩ vi suhamuvēnti garuāṇa ṇiaa-dukkhēhiṁ
rasa-bandhēhĩ kaīṇava viiṇṇa-karuṇāĩ hiaāiṁ // GaüḍVa.938 [āryā]

aṇṇaṇṇāĩ uvēntā saṁsāra-vahammi ṇiravasāṇammi
maṇṇanti dhīra-hiaā vasaï-ṭṭhāṇāĩ va kulāiṁ // GaüḍVa.939 [āryā]

sasiēhiñcia lōō dukkhaṁ lahuēi dukkha-jaṇiēhiṁ
āyāsa-kaēhĩkarī āyāsaṁ sīarēhiṁ va // GaüḍVa.940 [āryā]

paharisa-misēṇa bāhō jaṁ bandhu-samāgamē samuttaraï
vocchēa-kāarāiṁtaṁ ṇūṇa galanti hiaāiṁ // GaüḍVa.941 [āryā]

mūḍha siḍhilattaṇaṁ tēsaṇēha-vāsēṇakaha ṇu baddhassa
bāḍhaṁ gāḍhaarāaïjō iramottuṁtaṇantassa // GaüḍVa.942 [āryā]


[p. 140]
hōūṇa vi hanta ṇirantarāĩ dūrantarāĩ jāanti
ummōia-rasaṇantōvamāĩ ghaḍiāĩ lōassa // GaüḍVa.943 [āryā]

paḍhamaṁ ṇa guṇā guṇa-hēuṇō paraṁ tē taō saha guṇēhiṁ
sampaï tāṇa guṇaccēa ṇavara hā tē uṇa ṇa santi // GaüḍVa.944 [āryā]

kālavasā ṇāsamuvāgaassa sappurisa-jasa-sarīrassa
aṭṭhi-lavāanti kahiṁ pi virala-viralā guṇuggārā // GaüḍVa.945 [āryā]

thira-vāsaṇā-samutthā dōsā bandhāya ṇīa-cariāṇa
sappurisāṇaṁ caguṇā mōhāya ṇajhattiviramanti // GaüḍVa.946 [āryā]

ēsa virāō hiaaṁ jaṁ ramaï jahāgaēsu vihavēsu
ṇibbhacchaṇaṁ tu lacchīe ṇavarathira-maccharōrāō // GaüḍVa.947 [āryā]

so ccēa kiṁ ṇa rāō mottūṇa bahu-cchalāĩ gēhāiṁ
purisā ramanti baddhujjharēsu jaṁ kāṇaṇantēsu // GaüḍVa.948 [āryā]

kiṁ va sarūva-varo ccia sēvā-ṇindā-varo vva aha maggō
jaṁmahaïviñjha-vaṇa-gōarāṇa lōō pulindāṇa // GaüḍVa.949 [āryā]


[p. 141]
sariāō aṇēa-vihaṅgamāō tala-ṇimmalāĩ a vaṇāiṁ
māaṅga-kalaha-muhalā giriṇō a raïṁvirallanti // GaüḍVa.950 [āryā]

sīlēṇa jaï vivimalōtaha vi hu mā duggaaṁ jaṇaṁ chivasu
kālantara-ṇivvaḍiaṁ vasaïccia maṅgulaṁ tammi // GaüḍVa.951 [āryā]

kō tēsu duggaāṇaṁ guṇēsu aṇṇō kaāarō hōi
appā vi ṇāma ṇivvēa-vimuhaaṁ jēsu dāvēi // GaüḍVa.952 [āryā]

haraï parihīṇa-vihavassa ṇūṇa ṇia-paṇaïṇī vi appāṇaṁ
savvaṅgamasampuṇṇassa ghaḍaïkiṁjāmiṇī sasiṇō // GaüḍVa.953 [āryā]

hiaa kahiṁ pi ṇisammasukittiamāsāhaō kilimmihisi
dīṇō vi varaṁ ekkassa ṇa uṇa saalāe puhavīē // GaüḍVa.954 [āryā]

acchau tā vihaluddharaṇagāravaṁ kattha taṁ agaruēsu
appāṇaassa vi piyaṁ iarā kāuṁ ṇapāranti // GaüḍVa.955 [āryā]

gāḍha-maa-mūḍha-hiaā lahiūṇa dhaṇaṁ guṇaṁ va jaṁ kiṁ pi
kaha te bharihinti paraṁ appā vi hu jāṇa pamhusaï // GaüḍVa.956 [āryā]


[p. 142]
jaha pariayammi lōōtaha bhujjantō vi dukkaraṁ kō vi
pāṇi-sisirāĩ pāṇammi aṇṇahā hōntisalilāiṁ // GaüḍVa.957 [āryā]

bhūri-guṇā viralaccia ekka-guṇō vi hu jaṇō ṇa savvattha
ṇiddōsāṇa vi bhaddaṁpasaṁsimōvirala-dōsaṁ pi // GaüḍVa.958 [āryā]

sāmaṇṇa-sundarīṇaṁ vibbhamamāvahaï aviṇaoccēa
dhūmo cciapajjaliāhibahumaō surahi-dārūṇa // GaüḍVa.959 [āryā]

thōvāgaa-dōsaccia vavahāra-vahammi hōnti sappurisā
iharā ṇīsāmaṇṇēhĩtēhĩ kahasaṅgaaṁhōi // GaüḍVa.960 [āryā]

ukkariso ccēa ṇa jāṇa tāṇa kō vā guṇāṇa guṇa-bhāvō
sō vāpara-sucaria-laṅghaṇēṇa ṇa guṇattaṇaṁtaha vi // GaüḍVa.961 [āryā]

ṇavaraṁ dōsā te ccēa jē maassa vijaṇassasuvvanti
ṇajjanti jiantassa vi jē ṇavara guṇā vi teccēa // GaüḍVa.962 [āryā]

vavahāre ccia chāyaṁ ṇiēha lōassa kiṁ vahiaēṇa
tauggamōmaṇīṇa vijō bāhiṁ sō ṇa bhaṅgammi // GaüḍVa.963 [āryā]


[p. 143]
sama-guṇa-dōsā dōsekka-daṁsiṇō santi dōsa-guṇa-vāmā
guṇa-dōsa-vēiṇō ṇatthijē ugēṇhanti guṇamettaṁ // GaüḍVa.964 [āryā]

dīsaï sāmāanto vva kō vi hiaēṇa ṇimmalōtaha vi
hariañcia cūa-phalaṁ gaaṁ ca pariṇāma-paramatthaṁ // GaüḍVa.965 [āryā]

dīsanta-ṇimmalō jaï vi kō vi kajjēṇa ṇāsamō taha vi
piṅgaṁ pikēsaraṁ kuṅkumassa rāēṇa sāmaṇṇaṁ // GaüḍVa.966 [āryā]

saccaviāsaala-guṇaṁ pisajjaṇaṁ suvurisā pasaṁsanti
paḍibandha-ṇūmiaddhaṁ kō vā raaṇaṁ viārēi // GaüḍVa.967 [āryā]

sōhaï adōsa-bhāvō guṇo vva jaï hōi maccharuttiṇṇō
vihavēsuṁ va guṇēsu vi dūmēi ṭhiō ahaṅkārō // GaüḍVa.968 [āryā]

jēṇa guṇagghaviāṇa viṇa gāravaṁ dhaṇa-lavēṇarahiāṇa
tēṇa vihavāṇa ṇamimō tēṇañcia hōu vihavēhiṁ // GaüḍVa.969 [āryā]

daviṇōvaāra-tucchā vi sajjaṇā ettiēṇa dhīrēnti
jaṁ tē ṇia-guṇa-lēsēhĩ dēnti kāṇaṁ pi pariōsaṁ // GaüḍVa.970 [āryā]


[p. 144]
dūmanti sajjaṇāṇaṁ pamhusia-dasāṇa tōsa-kālammi
dāṇāara-sambhama-diṭṭha-pāsa-suṇṇāĩ viliāiṁ // GaüḍVa.971 [āryā]

saï jāḍhara-cintāaḍḍhiaṁ va hiaaṁ ahō-muhaṁ jāṇa
uddhura-cittākaha ṇāma hōntu tēsuṇṇa-vavasāyā // GaüḍVa.972 [āryā]

diṇṇaṁ purā jahicchaṁ taō a dēntēhiṁ saṇṭhiamabhāvā
gahiaṁ ca parāhintō taō a ō lōha-paṇaēṇa // GaüḍVa.973 [āryā]

lōē amuṇia-sārattaṇēṇa khaṇamettamuvviantāṇa
ṇiaa-vivēa-ṭhṭhaviā garuāṇa guṇā paaṭṭanti // GaüḍVa.974 [āryā]

gēṇhau vihavaṁ avaṇēu ṇāma līlāvahē vaya-vilāsē
dūmēi kaha ṇu devvō guṇa-pariuṭṭhāĩ hiaāiṁ // GaüḍVa.975 [āryā]

aghaḍia-parāvalambā jaha jaha garuattaṇēṇavihaḍanti
taha taha garuāṇa havanti baddha-mūlāō kittīō // GaüḍVa.976 [āryā]

āgama-lambhē vaya-pariṇaīebhaṅgēsudhaṇa-vilāsāṇa
thōvamasamañjasāĩ vi hiaāĩ vahantipariṇāmaṁ // GaüḍVa.977 [āryā]


[p. 145]
ṇa sahanti ṇia-guṇā ira puraō garuāṇa ia viintantā
ṇīāhigamē lahuā guṇāṇa bhāvañcia haranti // GaüḍVa.978 [āryā]

asalāhaṇe khaluccia alia-pasaṁsāe dujjaṇō viuṇaṁ
apavatta-guṇē suaṇō duhā vi pisuṇattaṇaṁ lahaï // GaüḍVa.979 [āryā]

appāṇa-ṇivvisēso tti ēsa mē jaṁ pi bhaṇaï ṇēhēṇa
taṁ pi khalō attha-gaīe ṭhavaï pisuṇattaṇeccēa // GaüḍVa.980 [āryā]

uvarimahō a dharantēhĩ kavva-kaṇaujjalē alaṅkārē
sīsaï sāra-visēsō vijjā-vihavāṇa savaṇēhiṁ // GaüḍVa.981 [āryā]

ṇa sirī calā mahagghēsu tē ṇa te ccēa sā vi jaṁ muaï
tē uṇa tē tañcia jaï muanti iha tīe kō dōsō // GaüḍVa.982 [āryā]

taṇhā akhaṇḍiaccia vihavē accuṇṇaē vi lahiūṇa
sēlaṁ pi samāruhiūṇa kiṁ va gaaṇassa ārūḍhaṁ // GaüḍVa.983 [āryā]

puraō sirīe piya-paṅkaāe kamalāaraṁ piva raanti
maṇṇē kiviṇā pahuṇō paṇāma-ghaḍiañjali-misēṇa // GaüḍVa.984 [āryā]


[p. 146]
kusuma-phalōsāria-pāavēhĩ viṇiatta-sauṇa-paṇaēhiṁ
taṁ kira ṇa maañcia mahiharēhĩ jalahiṁ visantēhiṁ // GaüḍVa.985 [āryā]

sōvāē suha-dukkhāgamammi ārambhiṇo phalamaïnti
cintā-ṇaha-kaṇḍū-sambhavammi vihiṇō ṇa kaṇḍuyaṇē // GaüḍVa.986 [āryā]

mōhāhibhavēṇa siriṁ cira-vōlīṇaṁ vimaggamāṇāṇa
dūrībhavantu āgantuāō kaha mā samiddhīō // GaüḍVa.987 [āryā]

āāra-pēsalāṇa vi havanti ēmēa vihi-ṇiōēṇa
viṇiattīo ccia āvaīō maṇṇē samahiletti // GaüḍVa.988 [āryā]

jammi avisaṇṇa-hiaattaṇēṇa tē gāravaṁ valagganti
taṁ visamamaṇuppēntō garuāṇa vihī khalō hōi // GaüḍVa.989 [āryā]

hiaassa viṇivvavaṇē iha lōe ccia samappia-phalāē
bīaṁ para-lōa-phalaṁ ṇa raṇṇa-vasahīe saddihimō // GaüḍVa.990 [āryā]

ramaï vihavī visēse thii-mettaṁ thōa-vittharō mahaï
maggaï sarīramadhaṇō rōī jīe ccia kaatthō // GaüḍVa.991 [āryā]


[p. 147]
mūlē ṇibiḍāantā viraluggārā taō pasaṅgēsu
kālēṇa saurisāṇa vi kahāṇubandhā ṇimillanti // GaüḍVa.992 [āryā]

virasāantā bahalattaṇēṇa hiae khalanti pariōhā
thōa-vihavattaṇēṇaṁ suhambharappaccia suṇanti // GaüḍVa.993 [āryā]

virasammi vi paḍilaggaṁ ṇa tarijjaï kaha vi jaṁ ṇivattēuṁ
hiaassa tassa taralattaṇammi mōhō iha jaṇassa // GaüḍVa.994 [āryā]

hiaammi gāḍha-ghaḍiēhĩ dō vi maṇṇē samaṁ ṭhavijjanti
buddhīō uhaya-lōammuhīō juvaīṇa thaṇaēhiṁ // GaüḍVa.995 [āryā]

paharaï kaha ṇu aṇaṅgō kaha ṇu hu vindhanti kōsumā bāṇā
ia kāme ccia aphuḍe phuḍāĩ tattō kaha suhāiṁ // GaüḍVa.996 [āryā]

hiaassa ṇiṭṭhurattaṇamiṇamō kiṁ saṇṭhavēhi mahilāṇa
attō payōharāṇaṁ vajjañcia vasaï ēāṇa // GaüḍVa.997 [āryā]

ramaï a cariē apphullaammi khijjaï a ṇiaa-sīlēṇa
ṇindaï a para-sahāvaṁ sihaï a lōō para-guṇāṇa // GaüḍVa.998 [āryā]


[p. 148]
magga vva dīha-dhavalā maṇṇē cihurā jaṇassa jāanti
vōlantāṇa aṇudiṇaṁ jahāgaaṁ hiaa-bhāvāṇa // GaüḍVa.999 [āryā]

savvaṅgaṁ viṇivēsō ṇaīi paliēhĩ ṇūṇa dāvēi
āsaṇṇamimammi jarā-karaṅka-bhāvaṁ sarīrammi // GaüḍVa.1000 [āryā]

savva-tthāmōṇamiaṁ ōhuramāaḍhḍhiaṁ vali-laāhiṁ
dharaṇi-alāhimuhaṁ piva sarīramiṇamōjarīvahaï // GaüḍVa.1001 [āryā]

aṅgēsubindu-ṇibiḍāṇivaḍaïpariṇāma-jajjarijjantī
tilaa-cchalēṇa maṇṇē kasaṇa-cchāya vva cihurāṇa // GaüḍVa.1002 [āryā]

gabbhuggama-laṅghia-jovvaṇāṇa ghariṇīevimaṇa-piya-diṭṭhaṁ
thaṇaāṇa duddha-dhārā-ṇihēṇa paliaṁ va ṇikkhamaï // GaüḍVa.1003 [āryā]

saalaṁ virāma-virasattaṇēṇa dukkhaṁ suhañcia ṇa ṇāma
dukkhābhāvō sokkhaṁ ṇa jēṇa ṇa hu tēṇa dukkhaṁ pi // GaüḍVa.1004 [āryā]

phuraï a phuḍō abhāvassa ēsabhuvaṇa-cchalēṇa āārō
ālōaṇa-ṇivvaḍio vva ṇīla-bhāvō ṇahaalassa // GaüḍVa.1005 [āryā]


[p. 149]
ia virasamimaṁ saṁsāramāvasantāṇa vo phalamamollaṁ
ṇivvaḍau pāvaṇāṇaṁ guṇāṇa pahuṇō ṇisamaṇēṇa // GaüḍVa.1006 [āryā]

avi a—

āsā-gaa-dāṇāanta-kasaṇa-kaṇṭha-ppahā-haō lahaï
kēsara-kalāva-karaṇiṁ so ccia siḍhilō jaḍā-ṇivahō // GaüḍVa.1007 [āryā]

vahaï maṇi-kiraṇa-rañjia-sīsa-ṇivēsia-phaṇā-samōsariō
bhuaïndō paṭṭhi-pahōli-ruddha-laṅgūla-vēlambaṁ // GaüḍVa.1008 [āryā]

tāo ccia rahasa-visaṭṭa-vaaṇa-kuharōarāō pāvēnti
jālāvalī-vilāsaṁ uttaṁsa-kavāla-mālāō // GaüḍVa.1009 [āryā]

paḍimā-maggāsira-sasialāe saccavia-ṇaha-muhōiṇṇā
te ccia hatthēsu ṇahaṅkusattaṇaṁ ēnti ṇintūṇa // GaüḍVa.1010 [āryā]

ia tuliumahilasantēṇa jassa bala-vibbhamaṁ ti-ṇayaṇēṇa
bhēsia-gōri-maïndaṁ maïnda-rūvēṇa pariṇamiaṁ // GaüḍVa.1011 [āryā]

khuḍiā imēṇasamaraṅgaṇēsuriu-vāraṇāṇakara-daṇḍā
ṇāsā-vimukka-jīhāha-ruhira-dhārā visahara vva // GaüḍVa.1012 [āryā]


[p. 150]
maha-dhūma-laā ēassa sucariāhūa-tiasa-ṇāhassa
sura-kariṇō bahala-maambu-sāmalā sahaï saraṇi vva // GaüḍVa.1013 [āryā]

lahuīkaā viguṇa-gāravēṇa garuā vi ṇiaa-kula-uvvā
appāṇa-gāravēṇaṁ puṇō vi guruīkaā jēṇa // GaüḍVa.1014 [āryā]

pahu-dhamma-bandhaṇē saṇṭhiassa vivarīa-sāsia-jaassa
karuṇā-ṇīsāsa-sahā sahanti saṁrambha-bhiuḍīō // GaüḍVa.1015 [āryā]

aha vā
kummāhivēṇa dīsaï uṇṇāmia-saṅkha-raaṇa-valaēṇa
tiasāṇa sambhamuggāhiaggha-vatto vva salila-ṇihī // GaüḍVa.1016 [āryā]

ummillassa vi cira-āla-mukka-ṇīsāsa-siḍhila-dēhassa
paṭṭhīpuṇōtaraṅgēhĩ laṅghiā kamaḍha-ṇāhassa // GaüḍVa.1017 [āryā]

dīsantikumma-tuliā ghaṇa vva puṇarutta-vijju-vipphuraṇā
ūsāsa-diṭṭha-tambira-kaṇṭha-cchēā mahā-mīṇā // GaüḍVa.1018 [āryā]

pecchanti sura-daïccā ghaḍia-dharā-magga-gōra-pariṇāhaṁ
paṭṭhiṁ pēranta-sahāva-sāmalaṁ kamaḍha-ṇāhassa // GaüḍVa.1019 [āryā]


[p. 151]
kumma-ṭṭhiassa dīsaï jalahimmi taraṅga-bhaṅgura-ṇivēsā
ṇa-pahutta-rasāala-kuñcia vva paḍimā mahiharassa // GaüḍVa.1020 [āryā]

valaïa-bhuaṅga-valayāvavīḍa-puñjia-ṇamanta-sāhaggā
aggēhĩ sēla-ghaḍiā mūlēhĩ dalanti duma-ṇivahā // GaüḍVa.1021 [āryā]

bhuaāhivassaṇihasājhijjanti urammi khara-harantīō
vaṇa-gaṇṭhi-gaāō vihaṅga-ṇāha-ṇaha-kōḍi-kīlāō // GaüḍVa.1022 [āryā]

phuṭṭanti pāavāṇaṁ raya-vitthārāvabaddha-parivēsā
viṇivatti-samaya-tāḍia-taḍāō pārōha-mālāō // GaüḍVa.1023 [āryā]

aṭṭhia-giri-valaṇa-gaāgaambu-vocchiṇṇa-ṇivaḍia-taḍāō
pattāō viaḍa-bhāvaṁ taliṇāōvi kaḍaa-sariāō // GaüḍVa.1024 [āryā]

parisiḍhila-viaḍa-mūlā te ccēavahantipaḍhama-taṇu-dhārā
bhuaïnda-ṇihasa-vihaḍanta-vivara-mūlā jaluppīlā // GaüḍVa.1025 [āryā]

vīsāma-mantharāanta-sēla-vocchiṇṇa-dūra-vaḍaṇāō
maḍahaṁ kamēṇa valayaṁ ṇijjhara-dhārāō bandhanti // GaüḍVa.1026 [āryā]


[p. 152]
pāvantivalia-vitthaa-giri-kaḍaa-ṇihaṁsaṇā taliṇa-mūlā
vitthāraṁ dasaṇa-cchēa-maṇḍalā diggaïndāṇa // GaüḍVa.1027 [āryā]

ṇihasa-virikka-duma-laō jaha jaha sēlammi ghaḍaï bhuaïndō
taha taha dīhāantō puṇō vi valaïjjaï girimmi // GaüḍVa.1028 [āryā]

ṇihasa-parigalia-vāsui-ṇimmōa-rayāvabaddha-parivēsō
kummammi hōi khaṇa-viraïālavālo vva salila-ṇihī // GaüḍVa.1029 [āryā]

kama-laddhālōaṁ phaṇi-ṇihaṁsa-jhijjanta-taḍa-paṇaṭṭhāsu
ṇinti a-viṇikkhamantā vivaṇaarā mahihara-darīsu // GaüḍVa.1030 [āryā]

hōnti giri-valaṇa-bhāvāaṇṇaṇṇa-disā-ghaḍanta-kaḍaāṇa
saralaṁ pi paḍantīṇaṁ silāṇa kuḍila vva gaï-maggā // GaüḍVa.1031 [āryā]

ucchalia-salila-pūria-gaaṇa-disā-valaya-paḍihaōāsō
khaṇa-tucchammi paḍiravō ṇavara samudde cciavalaggō // GaüḍVa.1032 [āryā]

vāsui-ṇihasummūlia-pakkha-cchēa-vaṇa-gaṇṭhi-ṇivvaḍiā
ṇivaḍanti sēla-kaḍaāō vajja-dhārā-taḍa-kkhaṇḍā // GaüḍVa.1033 [āryā]


[p. 153]
pasaranti valantōahi-maṇḍalaïjjanta-kaḍḍhia-sarīrā
suṅkāra-saraliāvatta-pasiḍhilāṇavarabhuaïndā // GaüḍVa.1034 [āryā]

taru-valia-laā-lacchiṁlahantisēlammikaḍaa-sariāō
ummōia-vāsui-ṇihasa-magga-sandāṇia-jalāō // GaüḍVa.1035 [āryā]

kaḍaēhĩ tahēa mahī-siharēhĩ ṇahaṁ va pelliaṁ giriṇō
allīṇaṁ ṇavara disāhĩ ṇihasa-taṇuammi majjhammi // GaüḍVa.1036 [āryā]

kumma-viṇihiṭṭha-mūlo bhuaāhiva-ṇihasa-taṇuiāhōō
kaha-kaha vi paḍhama-ṇimiō suhēṇaōsāriōsēlō // GaüḍVa.1037 [āryā]

ghaḍiaṁ mandara-dara-dūmiammi saṅkhuhia-jalahi-taṇṇāaṁ
sisirōvaāra-paṅkaṁ vakumma-vīḍhammi mahi-veḍhaṁ // GaüḍVa.1038 [āryā]

ia kama-ṇimmahiāmukka-vihura-khīrōa-sarahasuvvūḍhā
lacchī ajjavi vaccha-tthala-ṭṭhiā vubbhaï imēṇa // GaüḍVa.1039 [āryā]

kiṁ ca—

dīsaï kara-tāḍaṇa-mūḍha-ruhira-saṅgalia-sāmala-cchāyaṁ
hiaa-ṭṭhia-viraha-huāsa-dhūma-maïlaṁ va thaṇavaṭṭhaṁ // GaüḍVa.1040 [āryā]


[p. 154]
vaaṇuvvahaṇa-ṇivēsia-karuddha-ṇaha-maṇi-maūha-vocchēē
sandhantiṇirañjaṇa-ṇimmalāo thōraṁsu-dhārāō // GaüḍVa.1041 [āryā]

ghaṇa-lambālaa-mālā-ṇirōha-khaṇametta-puñjaïjjantā
umhavia-gaṇḍavāsaṁ cakkalaïjjanti ṇīsāsā // GaüḍVa.1042 [āryā]

ia līlā-rōsuggama-visamia-bhumaammi jammi vubbhanti
vēri-ramaṇīhĩ vēhavva-lambha-vihurāĩ aṅgāiṁ // GaüḍVa.1043 [āryā]

jassa muha-māruāhaa-visanta-bhuvaṇantarēṇa uarāō
vubbhaï va aṇṇa-bambhaṇḍa-ḍambarō pañcaaṇṇēṇa // GaüḍVa.1044 [āryā]

sō ēsakēsavō uvasamuddamuddāma-dāviāyāmē
aha sōhaïsēsammi vaṇiaammi jasammiviṇisaṇṇō // GaüḍVa.1045 [āryā]

aha vā
bhāruvvahaṇā-joggāarēṇa tārēhĩ ṇaha-maūhēhiṁ
sēsa-sisūhĩ va calaṇāravinda-ghaḍiēhĩ sōhantiṁ // GaüḍVa.1046 [āryā]

bhuaïnda-phaṇā-maṇḍala-ṇivēsa-paḍilagga-raaṇa-rāaṁ va
calaṇa-juamāvahantiṁ pajjattālattaa-cchāyaṁ // GaüḍVa.1047 [āryā]


[p. 155]
līlā-ghōlāvia-calaṇa-muhala-mañjīra-rava-milantēhiṁ
vubbhantiṁ sēsa-phaṇā-valaēhĩ va rāahaṁsēhiṁ // GaüḍVa.1048 [āryā]

kāraṇa-kiri-khandhukkhēva-lagga-parikavila-kēsara-cchāyaṁ
vahamāṇiṁ kiraṇa-kalāvamiriṇa-rasaṇā-guṇuggiṇṇaṁ // GaüḍVa.1049 [āryā]

sēvijjantiṁ sa-raaṇa-rasaṇā-paḍiṇivvaḍanta-paḍimēṇa
āḍhatta-rōhaṇuddalaṇa-vaïarēṇaṁ piva jaṇēṇa // GaüḍVa.1050 [āryā]

ṇāhi-vivarēṇa kāraṇa-varāha-dāḍhā-vahēṇa vasahantiṁ
pāāla-tamubbhēāamāṇa-rōmāvalīēṇa // GaüḍVa.1051 [āryā]

ajjavi aṇaha-ṭṭhia-rāma-ramaṇi-ṇiggamaṇa-sīra-maggaṁ va
uaramahirāma-vali-vīi-bhaṅga-visamaṁpaāsēntiṁ // GaüḍVa.1052 [āryā]

sōhantiṁ hārāvali-valanta-rōmāvalī-taraṅgēṇa
jauṇā-saṅgaa-gaṅgā-sottēṇa va majjhaēsēṇa // GaüḍVa.1053 [āryā]

lāyaṇṇa-paripphuramāṇa-pariaṇukkhitta-cāmara-caēhiṁ
antō-pāaḍa-bhūruha-mūla-kalāvaṁ va daṁsantiṁ // GaüḍVa.1054 [āryā]


[p. 156]
pahu-daṁsaṇa-rasa-pasaria-sasēa-rōmañca-sañcaya-ṇihēṇa
salilāhaa-dēsūsa[siaṁ] bīa-laaṁ va daṁsantiṁ // GaüḍVa.1055 [āryā]

antōvariṁ ca parisaṇṭhiēṇaṇaha-ṇiṇṇaāe va jalēṇa
paḍimā-paḍiēṇasiaṁsuēṇasaṁvalia-thaṇa-bimbaṁ // GaüḍVa.1056 [āryā]

kaṇṭha-kusumēsubahusō līṇuḍḍīṇēhĩ mahuara-kulēhiṁ
āyāsiaṅga-lēhaṁ savakkha-sēlēhĩ va puṇō vi // GaüḍVa.1057 [āryā]

muttā-pērantattaṇa-pāvia-pāāra-maṇḍala-guṇēhiṁ
divva-purēhĩ va maṇi-kuṇḍalēhĩ sambhāviābhōaṁ // GaüḍVa.1058 [āryā]

kuṇḍala-sasi-sūrantara-ṇisaṇṇa-kabarī-ṇisā-viṇīladdhaṁ
muha-maṇḍalaṁ sumēruṁ va kaṇaa-gōraṁ paāsēntiṁ // GaüḍVa.1059 [āryā]

savvattō hāra-maūha-daṇḍa-paḍiaggiaṅga-bhāvēṇa
ummilla-ṇimmalāṇēa-paha-samūhaṁ va dīsantiṁ // GaüḍVa.1060 [āryā]

avaaṁsa-kusuma-ṇīsandamāṇa-raa-bindu-kalia-mūlēṇa
gaṇḍatthalēṇadara-galia-rēṇu-bhāvēṇa va sahantiṁ // GaüḍVa.1061 [āryā]


[p. 157]
mālā-valaēhĩpaïṇṇa-surahi-kabarī-laaṁ mahuarāṇa
vēṇī-bandhēhĩ va bahu-ṇarinda-vēhavva-pisuṇēhiṁ // GaüḍVa.1062 [āryā]

ia suvvaï ēsō ira sarīra-bhāva-parisaṇṭhiaṁ bahusō
paccakkhañcia dēviṁ puhaïṁ pulaēi pīḍāsu // GaüḍVa.1063 [āryā]

kiṁ ca—

sīsaï va jassa tārāṇusāri-ṇiggaa-kalaṅka-valaēṇa
atti-ṇayaṇāhiajja vi samubbhavō ṇiaa-bimbēṇa // GaüḍVa.1064 [āryā]

vaṁsammi tassa raaṇī-ramaṇassa purā pariṭṭhiā pahuṇō
jē tāṇa aha paṇāmō ēsō uṇa kimpi ṇivvaḍiō // GaüḍVa.1065 [āryā]

avi a—

sajjhasa-saṁvēummīlaṇē vialasummuhā samuttaraï
diṭṭhī paharisa-viralāamāṇa-pamhantarālēsu // GaüḍVa.1066 [āryā]

tattōhutta-gaāgaa-hiaa-vahāanta-ṇaha-maūhēṇa
kara-kisalaēṇa lōlaṁsuammi thaṇa-maṇḍalē vasiaṁ // GaüḍVa.1067 [āryā]

gāḍha-jahaṇa-tthala-kkhalaṇa-muhala-maṇi-kiṅkiṇīamukkampō
paḍikusumandōlia-kaṇṭha-dāmamaṅgaṁ taraṅgēi // GaüḍVa.1068 [āryā]


[p. 158]
ia ṇivvattia-sejjā-pariṇayaṇāṇa paḍivakkha-kumarīṇa
jāanti jassa puraō sa-sajjhasā vammaha-viārā // GaüḍVa.1069 [āryā]

kēūra-maragaoggiṇṇa-kiraṇa-kalilēbhuammi appāṇaṁ
sā jassa viṇōēi va ṇaliṇi-vaṇukkaṇṭhiā lacchī // GaüḍVa.1070 [āryā]

ahiārāṇala-kuṇḍamba-maṇḍalaṁ tāva ṇaṁ samakkamaï
timiraṁ kulamiva tārā-phaṇa-raaṇavahaṁ visaharāṇa // GaüḍVa.1071 [āryā]

puhaī-vaïṇō amhē saccariāvēaṇammi kē tassa
suvvaï ṇa-pahuttañciatassa vi phaṇiṇō muha-sahassaṁ // GaüḍVa.1072 [āryā]

taha vi ṇisāmēha ṇarāhivassa bhua-dappa-dappaṇaṁ ēaṁ
raaṇi-viramammi ṇavaraṁ purumilla-ṇarinda-ṇiṭṭhavaṇaṁ // GaüḍVa.1073 [āryā]

sāhijjaïgauḍa-vahō ēsa maē sampaaṁ mahārambhō
ṇisuē muanti dappaṁ jammi ṇarindā kaïndā a // GaüḍVa.1074 [āryā]

ettāhē uṇa raviṇō uvvattia-kamaḍha-piṅgala-cchāō
parighōlaï vialia-kiraṇa-kandalō bimba-pariṇāhō // GaüḍVa.1075 [āryā]


[p. 159]
ēe chāyā-pariatta-muhala-pārāvaā pasajjanti
giri-kuñjuṇṇidda-maïnda-ṇandiṇō raṇṇa-pērantā // GaüḍVa.1076 [āryā]

maïlijjaï diasāhiva-kiraṇāiṇṇattha-sēla-galiēhiṁ
āyasa-rasa-visarēhĩ va chāyā-maggēhĩ mahi-veḍhaṁ // GaüḍVa.1077 [āryā]

sariāṇa ṇirantara-milia-vihaa-ṇivahōvarōha-muccantā
uvvellanti vaṇivvaḍia-maṇḍalā puliṇa-vitthārā // GaüḍVa.1078 [āryā]

dūrattaṇa-paḍhama-ṇiatta-gō-haṇā hōnti ṇaara-maggēsu
sālamba-diṇaaraccēa dhūsarā diasa-pariṇāmā // GaüḍVa.1079 [āryā]

thōamivaviaḍa-gamaṇā garuāanta-jahaṇālasamuvēnti
dhēṇu-dhavalīō paṇhua-pīṇāpīṇā vaṇantāō // GaüḍVa.1080 [āryā]

saṁvelliūṇa ekkaṁ diasārambha-paḍisāriaṁviñjhō
viiaṁ pakkhaṁ vapuṇōchāyā-valayaṁ pasārēi // GaüḍVa.1081 [āryā]

andōlaï diṇa-lacchī pacchima-sēla-tthalāvalambāsu
jaraḍha-sara-gaṇṭhi-rēhāruṇāsu ravi-kiraṇa-mālāsu // GaüḍVa.1082 [āryā]


[p. 160]
paccha-ṭṭhiāavattaṇa-suṇṇaïa-gavakkha-magga-païrikkā
jāā samujjalālekkha-sundarā mandiraddhantā // GaüḍVa.1083 [āryā]

taṁsāgaa-raviara-ṇivvaḍanta-mūlantarāla-viaḍāiṁ
viralāanti va chāyā-ṇiggama-siḍhilāĩraṇṇāiṁ // GaüḍVa.1084 [āryā]

sēlagga-khaṇa-vihattā ravi-vaḍaṇa-kamēṇadūramucchaliā
ghamma-cchēāivatāraattaṇaṁ ēnti maulintā // GaüḍVa.1085 [āryā]

ēnti gaha-mottiaḍḍhēpaōsa-sīhāhaē diṇēhammi
lhasia-ṭṭhia-ruhirāamba-kumbha-karaṇiṁ ravi-miaṅkā // GaüḍVa.1086 [āryā]

jāmavaī-muha-bhariē sañjjhā-maïrāe diṇaarāhārē
āāsa-kēsaraṁ danturēnti ṇakkhatta-kusumāiṁ // GaüḍVa.1087 [āryā]

āava-kilanta-mahisacchi-kōṇa-sōṇāavaṁ diṇantammi
uvvattaïraviṇo bhū-kalamba-puḍa-pāḍalaṁbimbaṁ // GaüḍVa.1088 [āryā]

sañjjhālattaa-dhariammiuaha jalaṇōvale vva ravi-bimbē
ṇivvaḍaï dhūma-lēha vva māsalā jāmiṇi-cchāyā // GaüḍVa.1089 [āryā]


[p. 161]
jāaṁ va dhūma-sañcaya-kalusāruṇa-kiraṇa-danturaṁ raviṇō
timirōvaāra-mujjhanta-visama-sañjjhāavaṁ bimbaṁ // GaüḍVa.1090 [āryā]

kālī-kaa-sarasa-gala-cchēa-mahā-mahisa-vibbhamō milaï
atthāambira-ravi-bimba-cumbiō timira-saṅghāō // GaüḍVa.1091 [āryā]

lahaï sa-sandaṇa-turaōtimirakkamanta-piñjara-sarīrō
mahumahaṇa-gāravuvvatta-piccha-garula-cchaviṁ sūrō // GaüḍVa.1092 [āryā]

jāēṇirāavē diṇaarammigiri-rēṇu-pāḍala-maūhē
ghōlaï milanta-timirā kulīra-kavilā diṇa-cchāyā // GaüḍVa.1093 [āryā]

ṇia-kara-kiliñca-ṇīḍatthamattha-giri-pāavāhi ravi-bimbaṁ
ṇivaḍaï sañjhā-kalalolla-vihaa-ṇāhaṇḍa-piṇḍaṁ va // GaüḍVa.1094 [āryā]

thōuvvattaṇa-lakkhia-sañjjhāruṇa-gaaṇa-tālu-pērantō
kavalēi paōsa-karī vihāṇa-piṇḍaṁ va ravi-bimbaṁ // GaüḍVa.1095 [āryā]

ṇaha-vaṭṭhaṁ dūruṇṇaa-sañjjhā-parivēsa-pariaraṁ sahaï
ahiṇava-paḍibandhāamba-bimba-viaḍāvaḍa-cchāyaṁ // GaüḍVa.1096 [āryā]


[p. 162]
purumilla-disā-gaa-timiramavara-bhāāvalambi-ravi-bimbaṁ
garulamiva gahia-gaa-kummamuaha paritambiraṁ gaaṇaṁ // GaüḍVa.1097 [āryā]

palhatthaï timira-mahā-varāha-paḍipelliō sumēru vva
sañjjhālōō paḍilagga-kēsarāanta-ravi-kiraṇō // GaüḍVa.1098 [āryā]

viaḍaṇḍammi va ravi-maṇḍalammi mukkammi paḍhamamaruṇaṅkē
ṇaha-siri-viṇaāe sasī vubbhaï vīaṇḍa-piṇḍo vva // GaüḍVa.1099 [āryā]

āsāra-pasara-saralā tālī-vaṇa-daṇḍa-dhūsarā hōnti
gandhavva-purāārā ṇirāavā ravi-ara-ṇivēsā // GaüḍVa.1100 [āryā]

rēhāvasēsa-diṇaara-maūha-ṇivvaḍia-daṇḍa-paḍibandhā
jālāaï sālōā avara-disā bhuvaṇa-bhavaṇassa // GaüḍVa.1101 [āryā]

gaaṇa-mahi-veḍha-ṇīlō majjhē sañjjhāvasēsa-paḍibhiṇṇō
ghōlaï khajjūra-kkhandha-pāḍalō timira-saṅghāō // GaüḍVa.1102 [āryā]

dīsaï disāsu tārā-saharī-jālāvilā timira-lēhā
ravi-paḍaṇa-sambhamārambha-rahasa-calia vva kālindī // GaüḍVa.1103 [āryā]


[p. 163]
sāyaṁ milanti kama-ṇivvaḍanta-tama-maṇḍalāvauṇṇāō
āsaṇṇa-bhāva-pāaḍa-ṇiaa-gaïndāō va disāō // GaüḍVa.1104 [āryā]

ūsasia-sāmalāruṇa-tama-vellī-mūla-lakkhiaṁ kōvi
gaaṇa-cchalaruṇayakañcamindubimbaṁ samuddharaï // GaüḍVa.1105 [āryā]

hōnta-vasuhāhiva-kahā-kōūhala-kaḍḍhiāō va milanti
diasa-virāma-cchavi-dhūsarāōsamaaṁcia disāō // GaüḍVa.1106 [āryā]

bahalattaṇa-kuharūsasia-tama-sihā-laṅghaṇōṇaucchaṅgā
dēnti thaluddēsaccia thōālōā darī-saṅkaṁ // GaüḍVa.1107 [āryā]

ālōō parighōlaï sasiṇo chāyā-ṇivēsa-vocchiṇṇō
maliṇāṇusāra-pasaria-kasaṇa-cchavi-magga-sabalo vva // GaüḍVa.1108 [āryā]

dīsaïṇisāsutārā-ṇihēṇa phuḍia-virala-ṭṭhia-kavālaṁ
bambhaṇḍagga-puḍaṁ pivakālantara-jajjaraṁ gaaṇaṁ // GaüḍVa.1109 [āryā]

jāāō kama-pasammanta-dhūma-raa-ṇiggamāvarōhāō
ārūḍha-paōsāō vi pavirala-timirāō va disāō // GaüḍVa.1110 [āryā]


[p. 164]
mūḍha-sasi-diṇaarālōa-majjha-puñjijjamāṇa-tama-kasaṇaṁ
sañjāamuhaa-dhārā-ṇimmala-khaggōvamaṁ gaaṇaṁ // GaüḍVa.1111 [āryā]

pērantēsu darābaddha-timiramōsukka-kamala-parisāmaṁ
ābhāi lāvaa-vahū-vaccha-kasāya-ppahaṁ gaaṇaṁ // GaüḍVa.1112 [āryā]

gaha-ṇivaha-bindu-sandōha-samia-sañjjhāṇalō samukkhivaï
uaya-supaṇṇō gaaṇammi amaa-kalasaṁ va sasi-bimbaṁ // GaüḍVa.1113 [āryā]

tama-mahuara-jāluppaaṇa-paaḍa-maa-maṇḍalaṁṇisā-vaïṇō
bimbaṁ māhavamiva piṇḍa-khaṇḍamāvāḍalaṁ uaha // GaüḍVa.1114 [āryā]

ukkhippaïgaaṇa-tulā-daṇḍēṇa samūsasanta-kara-kēū
pacchā ravi-piṇḍa-bharōṇaēṇa kalaso vva sasa-indhō // GaüḍVa.1115 [āryā]

saṁṇaddha-maaṇa-sāhijja-jāa-saṁrambha-pāḍalō ṇīi
parivēsa-cchala-maṇḍalia-cāva-valao vva hariṇaṅkō // GaüḍVa.1116 [āryā]

pāvaïuayāambō dara-siḍhila-kkhalia-taliṇa-tama-lēhō
lhasia-viṇīlaṁsua-matta-halaharāhaṁṇisā-ṇāhō // GaüḍVa.1117 [āryā]


[p. 165]
avi a—

takkhaṇa-kāmiaṇāṇia-mahu-casaōaraṇa-laddha-rāaṁ va
ubbhijjaï bimbaṁ saṅkha-ṇāhi-sōṇaṁ ṇisā-vaïṇō // GaüḍVa.1118 [āryā]

ūsasaï vilōla-karattaṇēṇa paṅkaa-viṇāsa-buddhīē
rahasummūlia-parilambi-bisa-kalāvo vvasasa-indhō // GaüḍVa.1119 [āryā]

ia jampiūṇa sayaṇāvalambiṇā tēṇa dēva-cariāṇa
āvēaṇammi appā a-pahuppanto vva paḍivaṇṇō // GaüḍVa.1120 [āryā]

jāo ccia kāavvē ucchāhēnti garuāṇa kittīō
tāo cciaataha-ṇivēaṇēṇaalasēntihiaāiṁ // GaüḍVa.1121 [āryā]

ṇavaria kē vāvārā pavaṭṭiuṁ paattā
kāmō vara-kāmi-aṇaṁ kēsara-uvvēhĩ bhindaï sarēhiṁ
iara-jaṇa-bāṇa-kajjammi kuṇaïhēyāĩkusumāiṁ // GaüḍVa.1122 [āryā]

kīe vi ahiṇava-bhumaā-ṇaḍāla-parisuddhi-laddha-pariṇāhaṁ
ahia-pihu-lōaṇa-juaṁ visēsa-tāraṁ muhaṁ sahaï // GaüḍVa.1123 [āryā]

vīābharaṇāa-kaaṇṇa-maṇḍaṇā ahiharanti ramaṇīō
suṇṇāō va kusuma-phalantarammi sahaāra-vallīō // GaüḍVa.1124 [āryā]


[p. 166]
gahia-vivihaṅgarāō akaañjaṇa-jhasura-mañjarī-raaṇō
pāvaïasamattālekkha-vibbhamaṁ kāmiṇī-satthō // GaüḍVa.1125 [āryā]

kōlīkaa-kālāaru-dhūmuppīla-cchalēṇa paḍihāi
ramaṇāhisāraṇē kāvi paharisāliṅgia-tama vva // GaüḍVa.1126 [āryā]

ūru-juaṁ malaya-bhavaṅgarāa-viṇivēsa-dara-samūsasiaṁ
guru-jahaṇuvvahaṇa-sahaṁ kaaṁ thōraṁ thaṇavaīhiṁ // GaüḍVa.1127 [āryā]

lakkhijjaï sīsē sarasamēva kaṇṭhē payōharumhaviaṁ
visamaṁ kusumābharaṇaṁ sama-kāla-kaaṁ pi juvaīṇa // GaüḍVa.1128 [āryā]

thaṇa-paḍimāgaa-pariṇīla-jāliā-maṇḍaṇaṁvarō ēi
vammaha-sara-saṅkā-hiaa-gahia-kavaaṁ vaṇava-vahuaṁ // GaüḍVa.1129 [āryā]

aviyōa-gamia-diasaṁsama-gahia-pasāhaṇaṁ paōsammi
sōhaï raāviaṇhaṁsayaṇāgamaṇūsuaṁ mihuṇaṁ // GaüḍVa.1130 [āryā]

galiummaūha-pihu-hēma-mēhalā-valaya-māliṇīkāvi
vammaha-bhayāhisandhia-sihi-pāāra vva paḍihāi // GaüḍVa.1131 [āryā]


[p. 167]
ṇa sahijjaï kāmi-aṇēṇa viraha-viaṇā-visaṇṭhulaṅgēṇa
sasiṇō ravi-maṇḍala-sampavēsa-tattaṁ va kara-jālaṁ // GaüḍVa.1132 [āryā]

jāāĩ dulaha-daïāṇurāa-raṇaraṇaa-mukka-thāmāṇa
taṇuāantāĩ vi kāmiṇīṇa garuāĩ aṅgāiṁ // GaüḍVa.1133 [āryā]

avi a—

paḍirōhi-kaṇṇa-pallava-paṇollaṇatthaṁ va tulia-bhumaaggā
agghaïṇimēsa-ṇiyamaṇa-phuranta-pamhāurā diṭṭhī // GaüḍVa.1134 [āryā]

ṇamaï ṇaḍālañcia lajjiēsu kara-malia-kaṇṭha-kusumēsu
uvvatta-pamha-cumbia-puḍāĩ ṇa hu ṇāma acchīiṁ // GaüḍVa.1135 [āryā]

hattho ghōlaï daṁsaṇasamaōsāria-ṇiriṅgi-viṇivēsō
bāṇīkaacchi-sandhāṇa-gahia-savaṇāvaāso vva // GaüḍVa.1136 [āryā]

lajjōṇaa-vaaṇālakkhiekka-dara-viasiāharantāiṁ
gamaṇammi vi ābajjhanti valia-majjhāĩ diṭṭhāiṁ // GaüḍVa.1137 [āryā]

ia kāmiṇīṇa piyaama-samāgamummillamāṇa-maaṇāṇa
sajjhasa-paḍibaddha-rasāĩhōnti līlāiavvāiṁ // GaüḍVa.1138 [āryā]


[p. 168]
lalaṇā vallahahuttaṁ vilāsa-bisa-maṇḍaṇāōvōlēnti
ṇīsaṅkañcia bandīkaïndu-kiraṇāo vva ṇisāsu // GaüḍVa.1139 [āryā]

sarasa-maa-tambimāhaa-kisalaya-mālāamāṇa-pamhāiṁ
ramaṇa-pavēsatthaṁ piva piyāṇa viasanti acchīiṁ // GaüḍVa.1140 [āryā]

avahīria-piyaamahutta-gamaṇa-bhaya-diṇṇa-saṅkhalāiṁ va
kajjalia-bāha-lēhāĩ hōnti kīē vi acchīiṁ // GaüḍVa.1141 [āryā]

thōēṇavi dūmijjaï ṇa lēi garuaṁ pi ṇāma-mantakkhaṁ
ia asamañjasa-hiaō hōi siṇēhēṇa juvaï-jaṇō // GaüḍVa.1142 [āryā]

valiuddha-kavōla-ghaḍanta-canda-bimbāṇa māṇaïttīṇa
antō dīsaï va ṇirōha-puñjiō hāsa-vicchaḍḍō // GaüḍVa.1143 [āryā]

sāsukkhaa-raa-lahuia-samūsasantuppalōṇaa-muhammi
casaammi kāvi parisēsa-māṇa-garuīcirāpiaï // GaüḍVa.1144 [āryā]

ahilāsā rahasa-viṇiggaēṇa kāmēsu-jajjaraṅgēṇa
kuvalaya-ṇālēṇa mahuṁ hiaēṇa va kāvi āpiaï // GaüḍVa.1145 [āryā]


[p. 169]
cira-saṇṭhiō vivialaïmāṇō cira-vialiō visaṅghaḍaï
vivarīa-rasaṁ kīlēimahu-maōkāmiṇi-aṇammi // GaüḍVa.1146 [āryā]

akhalia-sarīra-vaaṇōsahāva-hiaōsaranta-maa-dhīrō
matto tti ṇavara ṇajjaï kavōla-rāēṇa juvaï-jaṇō // GaüḍVa.1147 [āryā]

aṅgāĩ paaṇuāiṁ vi kimpi garuēi mahu-maa-vilāsō
hiaāĩ puṇō lahuēi māṇa-garuāĩ vi piyāṇa // GaüḍVa.1148 [āryā]

viraha-viṇiggaa-sēsa vva vibbhamā manda-hiaa-saṅgaliā
muha-ṇīsāsā piya-saṅgamammi sōhanti ramaṇīṇa // GaüḍVa.1149 [āryā]

sarasa-ṇaha-rāi-maggēhĩ pīṇa-thaṇa-maṇḍalāĩ taruṇīṇa
piya-saṅgama-harisūsāsa-rahasa-phuḍiāĩva sahanti // GaüḍVa.1150 [āryā]

sambhāvia-kāma-harōuppēi rasaṁasōumallō vi
ṇaha-rēhā-pharusa-payōharāṇa ramaṇīṇaparirambhō // GaüḍVa.1151 [āryā]

gāḍhāliṅgaṇa-taṇhā-ṇihēṇapaḍipīlaṇaṁ vapaḍivaṇṇaṁ
paḍhamaṁ kīe vi bhara-pīḍiēṇa hiaēṇa thaṇaāṇa // GaüḍVa.1152 [āryā]


[p. 170]
paḍhama-raārambha-rasāṇa vi taha vaccha-tthalōvaūḍhāiṁ
jaha pīḍia-jahaṇa-ṇirantarāĩ jāanti aṅgāiṁ // GaüḍVa.1153 [āryā]

accanta-maēṇa vilāsiṇīṇa parigalia-hiaa-suṇṇāiṁ
vaḍḍhanta-ṇīrasāĩ ṇasamappanticcia raāiṁ // GaüḍVa.1154 [āryā]

aṇṇōṇṇārāhaṇa-khaṇa-khalanta-hiaāvahīria-suhāiṁ
suhamabbhahiaṁraï-vittharēṇa pāvanti mihuṇāiṁ // GaüḍVa.1155 [āryā]

tāiñciakimpirasaṁ dēnti parūḍhē vipēmma-rāammi
piya-diṇṇa-ṇahāharaṇullasāĩ ramaṇīṇaramiāiṁ // GaüḍVa.1156 [āryā]

āvaaṇōru-ṇirantara-pīḍia-dēhāṇa haraï mihuṇāṇa
calaṇēsu vi kaa-calaṇō savvaṅgāliṅgaṇa-vilāsō // GaüḍVa.1157 [āryā]

thaṇa-bimbēsu vahūṇaṁ jovvaṇa-laddha-pariṇāha-viaḍēsu
so cciataha-pariṇāhōjāō viralo vva rōmañcō // GaüḍVa.1158 [āryā]

pīḍia-payōharōgāḍha-ṇaha-pauddēsa-dara-samūsasiaṁ
vimalaïkarēṇa ramaṇassa kāvi vaccha-tthalaṁ hasirī // GaüḍVa.1159 [āryā]


[p. 171]
bahuso bhagga-ṭṭhia-ramaṇa-ṇaha-sihā-cuṇṇa-viuṇa-garuēṇa
āyāsijjaï thaṇa-maṇḍalēṇa majjhālasā taruṇī // GaüḍVa.1160 [āryā]

taṇuattaṇa-ṇamiōara-payōharāsaṇṇa-jahaṇa-ṇimia-bhuō
sōhaï taṁsa-ṇuvaṇṇōvaliōru-laō piyā-satthō // GaüḍVa.1161 [āryā]

daïyāe kōvi ṇiddā-parissamubbhiṇṇa-sēa-binduiaṁ
pariumbaïsuha-ṇasahia-paḍibōhandōliaṁ vaaṇaṁ // GaüḍVa.1162 [āryā]

samabhāva-pavattūsāsa-siḍhila-ṇīsaha-pariṭṭhiāvayavō
dara-lakkhia-dubbalo vva hōi ṇiddāsu juvaï-aṇō // GaüḍVa.1163 [āryā]

ṇavaria ṇarinda-vikkama-viaḍa-kahāvasara-samuha-sura-mukkō
kusuma-ṇivaho vva ṇivaḍaï ṇahāhi tārā-lavuppīlō // GaüḍVa.1164 [āryā]

jāaṁ tārā-vaïṇō vāanta-muṇāla-pāḍala-maūhaṁ
bimbaṁ abāla-jambū-phala-bhaṅga-pisaṅga-parivēsaṁ // GaüḍVa.1165 [āryā]

ōsāriammi pacchā siṇhollia-timira-kēsa-hatthammi
ṇivaḍantisalila-bindu vva tāraā raaṇi-taruṇīē // GaüḍVa.1166 [āryā]


[p. 172]
lhasia-ṭṭhia-maa-vicchāya-majjha-sasi-bimba-cumbiaṁ sahaï
daddura-uḍaṁva dara-phuḍia-viaḍa-puḍa-maṇḍalaṁ gaaṇaṁ // GaüḍVa.1167 [āryā]

atthāa-taliṇa-tārattaṇēṇatañcēa paḍhama-pariviralaṁ
pacchā puñjijjantaṁpuṇō vi viaḍēi gaha-akkaṁ // GaüḍVa.1168 [āryā]

aruṇa-virāvia-taṇuāamāṇa-sañjjhā-rasāṇulittaṁ va
thōa-tthōamusālōa-paṇḍuraṁ hōi gaaṇa-alaṁ // GaüḍVa.1169 [āryā]

pamhantara-lakkhia-paṇḍu-bhāva-visama-ppahaṁ samuppaaï
siṇhā-haa-sāmāanta-masiṇa-dēhaṁkavōa-ulaṁ // GaüḍVa.1170 [āryā]

ārōhiṇā pahāa-kkamēṇa paripiñjarattaṇamuvēntā
viḍavēsu phala-visēsāpariṇāma-guṇaṁ va gēṇhanti // GaüḍVa.1171 [āryā]

mihu [ṇēhĩ raï]-rasāyāma-khēa-khaṇa-laddha-garua-ṇiddēhiṁ
paḍibujjhijjaï kaha-kaha vi sālasaṁ raaṇi-viramammi // GaüḍVa.1172 [āryā]

tama-lōha-loḍhaāṇugaa-mukka-gōsa-ppahō taliṇa-mūlō
gaha-palahi-bīa-ṇivahō pacchā puñjijjaï ṇisāē // GaüḍVa.1173 [āryā]


[p. 173]
āyāsēi paīvēsalōla-kajjala-sihā-daruvvattē
sa-kaa-ggahaṁ va paccūsa-māruō vāsa-gēhēsu // GaüḍVa.1174 [āryā]

tañcēa timira-maliṇaṁ jāaṁ aruṇa-ppahā-haaṁ gaaṇaṁ
sīsaamiva sindūrattaṇēṇa paḍivaṇṇa-pariṇāmaṁ // GaüḍVa.1175 [āryā]

gēṇhanti kaṇṭha-pharusāĩ kahavi raaṇī-jalāṇubhāvēṇa
vihaāvalagga-raa-saṁṇivēsa-garuāĩ bīāiṁ // GaüḍVa.1176 [āryā]

ruṇṇāruṇa-ṇayaṇāō va ṇisā-visūranta-ṇaliṇi-sōēṇa
sōhanti jalolla-ṭṭhia-cakkāa-juāō vāvīō // GaüḍVa.1177 [āryā]

sasiṇō samōsarantī atthāala-matthaa-ttha-bimbassa
sōhaï sahaāra-rasagga-taliṇa-paripaṇḍurājōṇhā // GaüḍVa.1178 [āryā]

asahia-visuddha-sukaāvaaṁsa-sappurisa-sucariuggārō
vivalāyaïkali-kālo vva bhiṇṇa-hiaō tamugghāō // GaüḍVa.1179 [āryā]

kōūhala-miliāmara-vimāṇa-raaṇa-ppahā-vibhiṇṇo vva
jāōajaḍa-javā-kusuma-pāḍalō ṇaha-ala-viāṇō // GaüḍVa.1180 [āryā]


[p. 174]
parigalia-paṇḍu-tārā-dalassa ṇaha-sāhiṇōviṇikkhamaï
ṇava-kisalaya-sōhaggēṇa paḍhamamaruṇuggamālōō // GaüḍVa.1181 [āryā]

iṭṭā-cuṇṇaṁ va kirantamuddhamaruṇāavaṁ paripphuraï
raviṇō gaaṇāsi-ṇisāṇa-cakka-valaōvamaṁ bimbaṁ // GaüḍVa.1182 [āryā]

jalahissa puṇō vi samāgamaṁ va bahalattaṇēṇa sūantaṁ
a-puṇāgamaṇāya va taṁ timiraṁ ummūliaṁ raviṇā // GaüḍVa.1183 [āryā]

ṇavaria ṇivvattia-raaṇi-virama-kāavva-ṇivvuō tāṇa
sō sāhiuṁ paattō cariaṁ cāṇakka-cariassa // GaüḍVa.1184 [āryā]

ṇavaria ṇivaḍia-tama-lōha-ṭaṅka-parisuddhi-tuṅga-viaḍāsu
āsā-bhittisu patthiva-pasatthi-joggāsu va ṭhiāsu // GaüḍVa.1185 [āryā]

agga-ṭṭhia-haria-turaṅga-pallavēmaṅgalāya kalase vva
takkhaṇamukkhittē taraṇi-maṇḍalē vāsava-disāē // GaüḍVa.1186 [āryā]

pahu-kitti-ṇisamaṇūsua-hiaa-kkhalia-ramaṇāhilāsāsu
andōliūṇa sura-sundarīsu rahasā viṇintīsu // GaüḍVa.1187 [āryā]


[p. 175]
kusuma-varisūsuāmara-vilutta-maṇi-maula-kandala-dalāsu
viralāantīsu surinda-mandirujjāṇa-vīhīsu // GaüḍVa.1188 [āryā]

amaodhaōa-parihiṭṭha-kaṇṭha-mahurīhuanta-rasiammi
maṅgala-jīmūa-ulammi gaaṇa-vaṭṭhē pauṭṭhammi // GaüḍVa.1189 [āryā]

caliammi rahasa-vialia-kaṇhāiṇa-ṇialiē muṇi-aṇammi
kōūhala-patthia-gaaṇa-hariṇa-paḍivaṇṇa-calaṇe vva // GaüḍVa.1190 [āryā]

viṇayāḍhatta-ṇarāhiva-caria-samāaṇṇaṇāarēṇaṁ va
āmukka-pāavāsaṇa-bandhēsu vihaṅgama-kulēsu // GaüḍVa.1191 [āryā]

lambi-mahā-dappaṇa-saṅkamanta-saṁmadda-ṇiravaāsēsu
bhavaṇa-kkhambhāvali-siharamāruhantēsu va jaṇēsu // GaüḍVa.1192 [āryā]

dhavalijjanta-samuṇṇaa-pahu-jasa-pāsāa-ghaḍia-mañcaṁ va
kama-lambia-tiasa-vimāṇa-maṇḍalaṁ ṇaha-alaṁ jāaṁ // GaüḍVa.1193 [āryā]

kiṁ ca—

tuha dhārā-sandāṇia-gaïnda-muttāhalō asījayaï
gauḍa-gala-cchēa-valagga-saṇṭhiēāvalīo vva // GaüḍVa.1194 [āryā]


[p. 176]
sama-jāittaṇa-sambhāviōvaārēhĩ ṇiaa-calaṇēhiṁ
pocchāhia vva calaṇē tu ēnti ṇialāvilā riuṇō // GaüḍVa.1195 [āryā]

kara-sandirēṇa sōhasi taddiasaṁ dāṇa-vāriṇā dēva
hiaa-bhariassa karuṇā-rasambuṇō ṇiggamēṇaṁ va // GaüḍVa.1196 [āryā]

ṇandaï tuha viṇiattassa āsamuddaṁ disāō jēūṇa
lacchī puṇō vi piuṇā sampēsaṇa-diṇṇa-vihava vva // GaüḍVa.1197 [āryā]

kārāsu paḍhamamaṇuhūa-ṇiala-mala-magga-lañchaṇācalaṇā
tae chēijjantiviiṇṇa-kāla-sutta vva sattūṇa // GaüḍVa.1198 [āryā]

saṅkanta-mahi-raō-dhūsarāĩsampaï tuha paṇāmēsu
bhiuḍī maïlaṇa-bhīa vva riu-ṇaḍālāĩ ṇāruhaï // GaüḍVa.1199 [āryā]

garuaara-matta-vāraṇa-khandha-samāruhaṇa-viraliēṇaṁ va
ūru-juēṇa virāaï sahāva-viaḍaṁ gaaṁ tujjha // GaüḍVa.1200 [āryā]

gheppaï aguṇīhĩ guṇi vva jēṇa guṇa-gāravēṇa vō appā
tēṇēa taṁ pi maṇṇasi appāṇamaṇajjia-guṇaṁ va // GaüḍVa.1201 [āryā]


[p. 177]
jāhe ccia taṁ calaṇōṇaāṇaavariṁkaraṁ pasārēsi
lacchī bhua-ṭṭhiā vō tāhe cciatēsusaṅkamaï // GaüḍVa.1202 [āryā]

akaōvaāra-taṇuāabhagga-pasarēsutujjha dīsanti
saṅkantā iva alaēsu kēsa-hatthā riu-piyāṇa // GaüḍVa.1203 [āryā]

iatāhe bhāvāgaa-paccakkhāanta-ṇaravaï-guṇāṇa
vivarokkhammi vi jāākaīṇasambōhaṇālāvā // GaüḍVa.1204 [āryā]

avi a—

aha suddhammi a ṇihasuttha-kañcaṇāharaṇa-raa-pisaṅgammi
jāammi suvaṇṇamae vva tammi jaṇa-saṁsiē diasē // GaüḍVa.1205 [āryā]

saṅkantāsēsa-sarassaïttaṇēṇaṁ va sāhirē tammi
jāōkhaṇēṇamūallio vvakōūhalā lōō // GaüḍVa.1206 [āryā]

kiṁ ca—

vīsambhamagantūṇaṁ va visama-mahilā-sahāva-dōsēṇa
bāhiñcia vēri-sirīō jēṇa paṇaīṇa diṇṇāō // GaüḍVa.1207 [āryā]

jassa viayāhisēē vivakkha-dēvīhĩṇava-ṇiōāhiṁ
pīāĩtakkhaṇūppia-camarantariāĩ aṁsūhiṁ // GaüḍVa.1208 [āryā]


[p. 178]
tassa imaṁpāvaṇamahiṇavaṁ cacittaṁ ca vimhaya-karaṁ ca
sīsaï cariamacaramaṁ ṇarāhivaïṇō ṇisāmēha // GaüḍVa.1209 [āryā]


kaïrāa-lañchaṇassa vappaïrāassa gauḍavahē gāhāvīḍhaṁ samattaṁ
